                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)  
Day of Remembrance  
<Prayer> Father, at this moment, your children scattered across the nation are worshiping before your altar. This is the time we offer our worship on behalf of this nation and people, responsible for the future and reality. May you preside over this time.  
In this complex world, are we truly the children you wish to have? How close are we to you in order to be with you? Please allow us to feel at this moment that you, as our Father, are saddened by our inability to stand in such a position.  
We must take the heavenly position as we move toward a single destination, following your command. This time is when countless angels and ten thousand saints praise your glory in your presence, and we pray before you, pledging to fulfill the mission of restoration that has been left to us.  
Father, may the praises of victory, honor, and glory be with you forever. No one knows that the foundation of victory you can preside over can only be achieved through the people of this earth, but we know this. However, when we, who know this fact, fail to achieve victory in the arduous journey of striving toward this goal, we cannot help but feel pity for the countless spirits in the spirit world.  
February 15, 1970 (Sunday), at the former headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).  
8   Day of Remembrance  
Human beings on this earth must prepare a day when they can overcome this and embrace the world, and we must realize that this is the final mission we must settle. Only then will the day you desire come. When we think of this, we understand that such a foundational result cannot be achieved without connecting each individual through emotional ties. We must once again feel how significant this mission is for us who stand in such a position.  
Father, who has toiled along the path of restoration that others do not know, we must realize that we should not regret or lament not discovering how our hearts can welcome the path presented by the countless ancestors in the spirit world who have traced the path of struggle.  
Father, we must now become a group that moves toward the purpose you desire and remain on this earth. Thus, we must become the substantial reality of heaven and the heavenly family that can forever sing praises before you in the name of goodness and truth. We have learned well that this is the case. When we feel that this substantial reality is none other than ourselves, we must overcome ourselves.  
We have longed for such a self. How much have we yearned for a family that can serve as a stepping stone to prepare the foundation of victory before you? Even if our appearance stands in a shabby and miserable place, we have started because of you, and we must remain on this earth as an individual and a family that can be connected with you.  
When this earth becomes a foundation where you can dwell and a solid ground where you can move, even if it perishes, it is not a true perishing, and even if it stands in a sad or miserable place, it is not a miserable place. We understand that this sadness and misery become the object of your comfort and the source of strength, laying the groundwork for us to run toward your will in the future.  
When we think that the resolution of the path you have come to find begins to unfold from here, even if we perish here, we wish to become not only a sacrificial offering before you but also a resurrected being. Thus, we will become the appearance that all of heaven and earth can bow down to as the offerings of holy history. However, we cannot help but discover that we are not able to do so.  
Father, we, who have not been able to do so, allow us to resolve in our hearts once again to become those who can.  
We have learned that you have walked the most miserable and pitiful path due to the bond of love that you cannot abandon us, your pitiful children. No matter how unjust and miserable we may be on this earth, we must voluntarily bow down and worship before you, who have endured until now with the joy of victory while standing on the boundary where you cannot feel the way.  
When our hearts are heavy and we call upon you with tears, how much do you long to meet your heavenly sons and daughters with tears, whom you have missed so dearly? How much have you longed for sons and daughters who can embrace you, hold your hand, and speak of their circumstances? When we think that your wish is for us to become a family that can be born in this world of enemies, we must understand that we cannot go to heaven without going through a family.  
We must go through tribes and nations, crossing over to the world, to reach the garden of your love, the eternal world of heaven. We must go through all these stages. Even if the path of asceticism lies before us, we must become those who do not mind the path of asceticism and join in this. No matter how thorny the path may be, we must fulfill our duty as children to follow the path you walk. We must encourage you, who are paving the way as a pioneer, even if our soles are wounded and we are in pain, and we must realize that we are those who must follow you with tears, worrying and comforting you.  
10   Day of Remembrance  
In the midst of the environment where enemies swarm, let us feel that we are the ungrateful ones who have never even dreamed that you are fighting against Satan to find everything for us.  
You have grown weary and have suffered in the battle against the world of Satan. Because of this, the steps you took to find us must have been even more arduous, but when we think of how we have never even considered your sorrowful heart until you came to find us, we realize how foolish we are.  
Your presence in such a fateful path is not because of your mistake, but because of our mistakes. We understand that your standing in a position of grievance and frustration until now is not your fault but the result of human error.  
We must bear hundreds of times the responsibility for this and pay thousands of times the price of sacrifice, but we must go until the day we can open the door to the garden of our original nature that we must go to. We must feel once again that there is a foundation of life there, Father, and we earnestly wish for this.  
Father, now we must realize where our hearts are directed and where our bodies are positioned. May we become those who can call upon you with a heartfelt desire to go toward you.  
We must become those who can call upon you with a heartfelt desire from the position of being all sinners before you, and we must bow down and shed tears with a longing heart for you. We must become those who can bear the cross of suffering that you have walked and can block the whip that strikes Jesus, who is bleeding miserably on the path of the cross, and take it upon ourselves. We must stand in a position where we can offer our lives as a stepping stone before your fateful path. Thus, we ask that you allow us to leave a history that we can commemorate as we build the heavenly world.  
Father, we must take responsibility for the world even if we abandon all material things.  
11  
We must create a path where you can manifest and embrace you, participating in the path you walk. Therefore, we must know what position we are currently in before you and understand how lonely and miserable your heart has been while enduring for us until now. How many times have we betrayed you? We have been so bold. We have called upon you from a very Cain-like position. When we think of this, we must realize that no matter how good we are, we cannot uphold our dignity and face.  
Today is a holy Sabbath. Father, please remember your sons and daughters gathered here. The path we take for heaven is lonely and sad, but there are your children who are struggling to establish the traditions of heaven, so please remember them. May you share in their loneliness and their difficulties. When they fight in lonely places, may you fight alongside them and encourage them. When we think of how much you are laboring for those who walk alone in a world unknown to others, we realize how much you are working for them.  
Father! There are those who kneel and offer their sincerity, saying that Korea is the country where the True Parents live, so please do not forget them. We must clearly realize that this is the foundation of true love and justice.  
Father, we must not forget that they are in miserable positions. If we do, we must be ashamed of ourselves. We, who are at the headquarters of the Unification Church, are struggling to walk that path, but we feel pity for ourselves as we struggle to overcome nations, peoples, and the world. However, we earnestly wish to become your children who can feel how unworthy we are before those who are fighting for the will abroad.  
Today is a holy Sabbath. We know that there is an unforgettable day of remembrance left from exactly two years ago. We understand that you have toiled on the path of trials that no one knows to establish us on this earth. We thank you for allowing us to think of the path of adversity during this hour. We sincerely thank you for allowing us this time to commemorate that day with gratitude and to express our appreciation for your efforts and grace in finding us until now.  
Though the teachings you have given seem to flow away, we thank you once again at this time for asserting that they remain on this earth, piled upon history, and become the foundation of victory before this nation and the world. We raise our hands and shout for joy. During this time of prayer, shedding tears to convey your will, we earnestly wish for your blessings.  
People always find it easy to live centered around themselves. We know that the desire to avoid lonely paths is also for the sake of centering on oneself. Though humans cannot think of others without thinking of themselves, we must stand in a position where we think of you, Father, without thinking of ourselves.  
Though we are distant from you and our situations differ, we always earnestly wish to stand before you from a holistic perspective.  
Whenever we think that we cannot hide our shameful appearance before the will, we earnestly wish to become your sons and daughters who can reflect, Father. Just as this day was necessary to give birth to a new day, we earnestly ask that we become a substantial group that the world needs, desiring a new generation today.  
We earnestly ask that you be with your sons and daughters who are active around the world today, and we offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.  
<Words> Every person living on this earth, regardless of who they are, wishes to leave a moment in their lifetime that they can boast about regarding their environment, country, or the world. This is the nature of humans living on this earth.  
From immature children to adults, everyone lives with such thoughts. And this is the beginning of human life.  
So when will the days of remembrance that one can have actually arise? They will appear during extremely miserable times, during times of suffering, and during moments of joy.  
The desire to leave a day of remembrance is the nature of humans.  
If there is someone walking the path of suffering for the world, the day when miserable things happen during that process will remain as a day of remembrance for that person. For someone living a happy life, the happiest day among that happiness will become one of their days of remembrance.  
However, most ordinary people do not think of their days of suffering as days of remembrance. They likely think of the moments of joy and happiness in their lives as unforgettable days of remembrance. This is true not only for people living on this earth today but also for those who will live in the future.  
Today, many people say they are making efforts to leave days of remembrance, but we, living in a fallen era, must seek a new world from the perspective of the present age. Can we truly have days of remembrance that leave a foundation of joy? This seems impossible even when considering the flowing trends.  
Everyone knows that the current world is a chaotic one. Humans are in a reality where they have lost their direction and cannot even clearly identify themselves. Given this, it is impossible to have days of remembrance that can be left with joy throughout one’s life on this current stage. No one can deny that humans are in such an environment.  
From this perspective, at this historical moment today, no matter how good the environment may be…
Even if one has a day to boast about, it is impossible for that day to be remembered as a day of joy on the world stage or the national stage. Then, if there is a day of memory that humanity today can universally embrace on the path that humans must take, what kind of day would that be? We cannot deny that we are in an environment where the whole must face a miserable day rather than singing about a day of happiness.

We must have a day of memory centered on God and marked by historical significance. So, for whom should that miserable day become a day of memory? This is the question. Will we celebrate that day as a day of memory for the Republic of Korea, or as a day of memory for numerous nations, or will we embrace it as a day of memory centered on God? 

Looking at it from a small perspective, there may be a day of memory centered on myself, but even if such a day remains, it cannot boast in front of a day that the nation can remember. Furthermore, even if there is a day of memory that the nation can boast about, it cannot boast in front of a day that the world can remember. Moreover, even if there is a day of memory that the world can boast about, that day will inevitably lose its value in front of a day that can be remembered by God centered on the universe.

The history that has flowed in this universe is destined to present a certain time and leave a certain time behind. Then, what kind of day must that day of memory be in order to be left behind? When considering this issue, there may be many who wish to leave a memory centered on themselves in the world. However, even if one has left a day of memory centered on oneself, that day cannot relate to the tremendous days of memory that nations and the world possess. In other words, those who seek to have a day of memory centered on themselves will only become a condition of sorrow in the process of seeking a global day of memory. When we look at this issue, we must conclude that anyone who wishes to center everything around themselves and leave a day of memory is a foolish person.

From this perspective, if there is a day in the historical age or in this world and universe where all humanity and God can truly celebrate a victory together, when would that day be? Will that precious day of memory come suddenly, or will it come through some process of connection? That day will not come suddenly.

A day of memory must encompass the memories of a day, a year, a decade, or even a lifetime, and must go beyond the memories of countless races, nations, and the entire world in order to represent history, the times, and the future eternally.

Then, who should that day be centered around? It must not be centered solely on humanity. It must not be centered on the 3 billion people living in today's world. Even if a day of memory that the 3 billion people can all rejoice in is determined, if it does not carry historical significance, it will simply pass by. If there are those who boast about a day of memory that cannot be a historical day of memory, we must understand that such groups will inevitably be judged in front of a historical day of memory.

What we must understand today is that we must leave a day of memory along with history. It should not be a day of memory centered on a single nation, but a day of memory that leaves a mark alongside the world and flowing history. We must recognize this issue. Therefore, we cannot deny that humanity must follow the path to leave a day of memory along with history.

Leaving a day of memory that humanity's history can commemorate is the path of destiny that follows our intentions. Then, can a day of memory centered solely on humanity remain forever? There must be an absolute subject. When that subject is God, He must intervene in the history that flows today centered on humanity. He will manifest Himself. Therefore, even if humanity has a day of memory that can remain in history, if it does not have the content to connect with the historical era centered on the absolute God, it cannot remain forever. Thus, no matter how much one boasts about having a historical day of memory representing humanity, we must understand that it will inevitably become an object of judgment in front of a day of memory that relates to God.

The important issue here is to leave a foundation of memory that can be centered around God in individuals, families, societies, nations, and the world. This is perhaps the most important thing. Those who have fought with their lives to pursue a day that can leave such a foundation in history are the saints who have appeared throughout history. Their teachings were to introduce God and the character of God. They are those who have walked the path of labor to connect human hopes with God's hopes. Therefore, we must understand that this is why they could remain in the ranks of saints.

What can be the motive for memory? The path to laying such a foundation of memory is not today’s business, nor politics or culture. It is religion. Although people generally dislike religion, we cannot help but think that finding the foundation behind that religion is what will leave a day of memory that heaven and earth can commemorate.

When you look at a family, it is not enough that the house is nice and the surrounding environment is good. Conversely, no matter how poor the environment and how shabby the house, if it becomes a refuge and connects all of one's stories, life, and standards there, that is a good family. There is a heart of mutual care between parents and children. This is the homeland of memory and the motive of all life, which becomes the foundation that governs happiness in our lives.

Why is that? It is because there is a unique bond of love between parents and children that cannot be violated by anyone, and there is a blood relationship of love that exists only once between parents and children. Because love between parents and siblings serves as the motive, it connects to the object of longing in our lives. Therefore, in that place motivated by love, when there is joy, that joy will manifest as the joy of the whole, and when there is sorrow, that sorrow will manifest as the sorrow of the whole. The entire atmosphere will unify at once. Such a place is the object that everyone pursues.

Therefore, to rejoice in such a place, to grieve in such a place, and to make a new resolution in such a place will be the motive that can bring about new results for that person. Even in the path of miserable trials, one can expand the foundation to overcome the enemy. All these facts can be understood through the phenomena and lives that have appeared in society as we have passed through the historical age.

From this perspective, a family must have the content of memory that can be pursued externally, that is, in terms of environment.

So, what can be the motive for memory? The bond of love centered on the relationship between rich and poor can be the motive for memory. The joy in that family is not the joy of one person, but the joy of the whole, and when there is misery, that misery is one that the whole must resolve together. This becomes the requirement for a memory that can remain forever.

In other words, if there is an enemy to the parents, the children cannot walk the path they must take until they repay that enemy throughout their lives, and they cannot live their own lives. Such a life is the memory that is bound closest to the heart. Even though it is bound in one, it contains the content that can govern the fate and life of the whole, and you must understand this.

When we look at the relationship between God and humanity today, we are confronted with God's intentions. If there is someone who can shed tears on behalf of the nation and the world with God's ideals in such a position, that person will be forever remembered by God and will not be forgotten by humanity. Moreover, in the process of pursuing the world of purpose centered on God, we cannot deny that the history that such a person has walked will remain as a day of memory.

What is religion? In today's world, religion has appeared to replace the form of family. 

You are likely familiar with the parable of the prodigal son in the Bible. You can see many unfilial children in the world. If there is a way to make such unfilial children or the prodigal son repent, what would that path be? Parents cannot make the prodigal son repent by having a lot of money and forcing him to submit to that money. The way for the prodigal son to repent and become a new human being is to constantly confront the love of the parents. When he feels that love is higher and deeper than heaven and earth, and feels that the parents are alive, he will finally come to appreciate the inherent value of love. Here, the love that operates becomes joy.

Here, a new human being is sought, and here a new family can begin, and a new nation and a new world can manifest. In other words, through the emergence of a new movement, it becomes the motive to form a new family, and when that new family is born, it becomes a tribe, and when that tribe grows, it becomes a nation, and when the nation grows, it becomes the world.

Such historical connections have not been left by the political society that appears in today's reality, but rather by religion in human history. Even if one goes the path of death for the sake of comrades beyond their own life, they can only be found in religion. This is an undeniable fact that we can know through history.

Religion has become the motive for human paths and the origin of new cultural creation. When we look at all historical facts, we must recognize that religion is the motive for everything. Even when we look at the background of world cultural history today, we see that it has been built upon religious thought, and that the history of that country has been sustained by it. Because the content of emotional connections of memory resides here, we must understand that history has taken shape in the world on this foundation.

Therefore, today, all humanity wants to recognize the true sacrifice that religious leaders faced in their pursuit of the path of truth and to celebrate that day as a day of the world. If there are sons or daughters who have sacrificed for the will of their parents, how much would those parents want to remember the sacrifice of their children as a scene of memory?

God also has such a heart and such a demand. Therefore, we cannot deny that religion remains as an object of memory and reverence in the historical process. Moreover, Christianity has woven a path of martyrdom more than any other religion. What was the center of that martyrdom? It was not centered on oneself, but on the will of God. For the world that humanity must ultimately seek, many people shed the blood of martyrdom for the sake of establishing a foundation upon which God can anchor peace on this earth and for the original peace of humanity.

From this perspective, what can be remembered in the history of religion is the countless loyal patriots who died for the purpose of that religion. It is through this that religion develops and achieves its purpose. Therefore, we cannot help but remember those who were sacrificed in the process of development.

When viewed through the lens of Christian history, Stephen was an ignorant person. At that time, no one could follow Jesus. In such an environment, he was chased and stoned, sacrificing his one and only life for Jesus as if it were nothing. However, the death of Stephen itself is not great. The fact that his life’s bloodline was cut off means nothing, but the greatness of his death lies in the fact that it was connected to God's heart and linked to history. Thus, through the shedding of blood centered on historical connections and emotional content, it became stained in history and in God's heart. Therefore, as humans who cannot go without washing away this blood, God must show this path, and humans on earth must not fail to commemorate it. We must understand this.

Then, do we have a person we can commemorate in world history, or a nation, or a family? Or are we an individual who can do so? This is the question.

We must desire a place where we can leave memories. If one can hold onto a family and leave memories rather than just focusing on oneself, that person is happier. And if one can leave a moment of memory centered on the nation rather than just the family, that person is greater than one who has left memories for the family. Furthermore, if one can leave memories that heaven and earth can recognize, transcending the nation and the world, that person will join the ranks of saints. Even if that person falls miserably on this earth and leaves no basis, they will remain with the world and will not perish.

Consider how Jesus left a day of memory. He was in a position like a fisherman by the Sea of Galilee. He lived by going from village to village, often receiving disdain and bad reputations from the townspeople. 

It should not be the case that he dies on the cross at Golgotha. However, how did his death become a foundation for establishing a democratic world that governs 20th-century civilization? This is the question. Anyone can die shedding blood. However, what is uniquely different about Jesus is that he died as a definitive memory that humanity can universally commemorate.

In other words, he took with him more of God's heart than anyone else. Although Jesus, the Son of God, shed blood and died, when we look for the path he left behind, the content of Jesus' ideals centered on God is clearly revealed to have historical significance. Because the emotional foundation of Jesus became the source of history, humanity has longed for that source until now.

Because this has remained as a foundation that can become the leaven of history, when humans who are heading in one direction centered on God encounter that foundation, they will automatically be influenced, and the purpose will be reestablished from individuals to tribes, from tribes to nations. Thus, the thought of Jesus centered on Christianity has created a global cultural sphere.
You must understand the thread.
Although it may seem that the death of Jesus is nothing, through it, Jesus stood at the pinnacle of the heart that could connect heaven and earth, which had never existed in history. He called God His Father and declared Himself to be God's only begotten Son. This is what makes it great. At the same time, as a son, He fulfilled filial piety for the will of the Father and devoted Himself to His kingdom. Therefore, Jesus is the ultimate filial son before God in human history, and God could finally proclaim Him as His only begotten Son. Jesus left behind the ideology that He would start the victory through filial piety.

Today, those who do not believe in Jesus do not even seek to know whether Jesus came to this earth 2,000 years ago, but those who believe in Him mourn His death and commemorate His life. Is it not a reality that they shed tears while truly commemorating Him, saying that the Lord sacrificed for humanity? Then why did Jesus stand in a place that history cannot reach, or a time that the era cannot touch? In other words, why did He stand in a place where even the sovereign of that nation could not go? It is because He called God His Father and declared Himself to be His Son, seeking a heavenly family. Thus, Jesus left behind the content of memories along with that will.

Every religion has such a foundation of memories. Therefore, we can understand that the deeper, broader, and greater the content that a follower of any religion can sacrifice their body for that will, the more that religion becomes a global religion.

Today, humanity around the world is facing the brink of life's adversities. However, even in this world, there must be a point in our lives where we can leave behind memories. In other words, in this reality where the complex waves of death are swirling, there must be a religion that allows us to hope for rest in the depths of our hearts. From this perspective, we, as humans today, are in a position where we cannot find our existence unless we do not deny reality while looking ahead.

Deny reality in the true sense.
Even the youth in such an environment must not deny reality to achieve happiness in their future. So, do they deny for the sake of something valuable and to leave behind a memory? No, they are like a swarm of locusts that do not know the direction. They are like a swarm of locusts flying from one desert to another without being able to fly in the grasslands. If there is no guide before their will, they cannot discover the grasslands and end up collapsing all at once like a swarm of locusts.

Therefore, they must stand in a position where they deny all such realities rather than leaving behind something that can become a memory in the place where they live and create a foundation for memories in the future world.

Religious people have denied reality from the past to the present. They have denied their own country. Even if they have their own ethnicity, they could not love that ethnicity as their own. Even if they have their own family, they could not make that family a foundation for their rest. Furthermore, as individuals, they have not been able to possess the authority to hold the entire universe. That is why religion started from complete denial.

However, religious people have not been able to establish a connection with that denial. They should seek the factors of happiness from the values beyond that denial, but because they have entered a habitual realm of denial, they could not unite with the foundation of happiness. However, if a standard can be established that can truly deny, new solutions will be sought in religion.

In this sense, today, the Unification Church must contribute to this realistic world.

When I think of the title "Day of Memories," I recall May 20, exactly 21 years ago. What day was that? It was the day I was taken to the Pyongyang Police Department, tried, and transferred to Hungnam Prison. Seeing this, you, who know the will, must ask yourselves what you need to find in order to align yourselves with the teacher. If you approach it with an ideology that comes from ordinary or common life, it will just flow away.

If the Unification Church has left a certain origin as the Unification Church until now, what kind of day is that memory day that resides behind it? It is not a day of memories left by you when you entered the Unification Church. You must understand that. This day of memories must be a day that can remain with the Unification Church. It should not be a day of memories centered around oneself but a day of memories that can remain with the Unification Church.

Then, when we say that the Unification Church has history, what is the background of that history? What kind of dimensionality does it have, and what kind of memories does it possess that no one can deny? This is an important issue. It is related to whether the future world can be moved or not. Also, regardless of how limited the environment may be, there is the issue of how a representative can connect the world before God with what content. This will become the foundation of memories for future generations of the Unification Church.

So, will you walk as happy members of the Unification Church? I do not think so. When thinking about the Unification Church itself, one might say that if you enter the Unification Church, you will eat well, live well, and receive more blessings than anyone else. However, that is not the case. You must have a history of memories that can illuminate the heart of humanity and show explosive driving force to recreate a new human being. That must become a foundation through which individuals can make new resolutions and new commitments to move toward a new purpose.

The days of memories left by the Unification Church.
The Unification Church does not always have only green spring days. When spring passes, summer comes; when summer passes, autumn comes; and when autumn passes, winter comes. In spring, new buds sprout, and in summer, flowers bloom, but this itself is not completion. If there are branches that extend sideways from here, they must be cut off. The fortune that extends must be cut off so that the autumn season can come with fruition. It means that what has spread must be denied.

You must achieve the four-position foundation. The world of existence must reproduce. Also, if there has been development, it must necessarily be reduced. It is like entering the winter season after autumn passes, like the cold of the three-month winter.

Unification Church members must have the power to repel anything that intrudes externally. Only then can they embrace the authority of heaven and earth and welcome the spring days in harmony with heaven and earth. When they can strengthen the power to achieve life, they can burst out all inner pain and achieve external victory. The memory of this one day when the Unification Church can rejoice is established in the relationship with God. This is something only we can do.

What I am grateful for is that although the path the Unification Church has walked has been miserable until now, it has not avoided this misery even when it reached its extreme. It has fully accepted that suffering. Moreover, it did not just accept it but accepted it along with heaven and earth. There is significance in this.

In a position of a parent-child relationship, we shed tears and resolved to hold each other for the sake of a new nation. This is not a place of destruction. It is a place where hope for tomorrow is found, and new life begins. Even if the path of the Unification Church is miserable, the Unification Church will not perish. Even if that misery increases in that place, by becoming a sacrifice that can embrace this nation or the world and bind the hope for tomorrow, life force is interwoven, and we will not perish. We must not be pessimistic just because we feel we have nothing. History starts from such places toward a new direction.

What kind of memories do you want to leave in history?
We have gone through thousands of years of history, but humanity has never had a day to rejoice freely. They have not had a day when they could dance joyfully, believing they are happy.

Therefore, we must leave behind a foundation of memories that can move history. In light of this issue, we must embrace God's heart in the content of sorrow rather than joy and struggle to enter into God's inner heart, resolving to face the path humanity must take in the future. While gazing at the reality of the world of enemies that is collapsing, moving toward the hope of tomorrow, which is heaven, is the profound memory that the Unification Church possesses, and that place is a precious place that cannot be exchanged even for heaven and earth. Without this connection, even if God gives us heaven and earth, we cannot inherit it. Thus, this is more precious than anything else.

Then, what kind of memories do you want to leave in history as you have walked until now? If there is a woman, will you leave behind memories that you can rejoice with her? Or will you leave behind memories that you can rejoice with your brothers, or will you leave behind flat memories among humans? No. You should desire to leave behind memories that are dimensional, centered on eternity, and can seek eternity, for the one purpose. Even if I forget this day and do not remember it, I must leave behind a day of memories that God can remember. This is the issue. Even if I forget all the days of my life, I must leave behind a day that God can ask me to remember through me. If so, he will not perish.

Such a person is greater than a king who rules millions. This is because even if a king passes, the history of such a person remains. Even if the king of that nation passes, a patriot with memories that can remain in history governs history.

From this perspective, if there is a person who has a day of memories that can be commemorated before God, who is the Lord of heaven and earth, or God, who is the King of kings, that person will be left in the historical process. That person cannot perish. Even if there are conditions that can lead to destruction, we must understand that they can be transformed into factors for prosperity.

Then, today, dear members of the Unification Church, can you leave behind a day of memories that you can be proud of in your life? This is an extremely important issue. In leaving it behind, it must become a day of memories that God can commemorate. Otherwise, no matter how many days you commemorate as days of memories, God will not cooperate with this. That day will just flow away. However, if you leave behind a day that God can establish as a day of memories, even if you forget that day, you will not perish along with that day.

Leave behind a day of memories with God.
What is it that the teacher is concerned about when celebrating and commemorating certain days along the way? It is whether these days will not just flow away but will truly be days that God can commemorate before I commemorate them. God has not been in a joyful place until now. God, who has woven a miserable history, has been in a place more miserable than anyone else. Therefore, if you want to leave behind a day of memories while walking the path of heaven, you must be able to leave it behind from a place even more miserable than that. You must understand this fact.

You must overcome whatever trials and pains come your way in the future. You must recognize that the path you must face is the path of your inherent destiny and be able to fully embrace it. I am sharing these words with the hope that you can leave behind a day of memories with God in the journey of your life.

This can only be left behind if you feel the mission of being the sons and daughters of the Father centered on God. When we realize that this path is nationally close before us, we must understand that there is a day of memories that can be left in the path of restoration, where we can leave behind the time of victory with God.

**The Messenger and the Homeland**

We know well that we cannot achieve a new history by settling in a realistic position. This is because no new revolution or innovative movement can arise from a position that aligns with the existing world's trends or ideologies. Therefore, we must completely deny the ideologies or trends of the existing world and have a hope for a new future, equipping ourselves with new achievements to weave new developments.

As we look at the historical process, this fact cannot be denied by anyone.

Just as the historical development of this fallen world is the same, our providential path is also the same. This providential path is not aligned with the direction of the satanic world and does not share its content; rather, both the direction and content are entirely opposite. From this standpoint, how difficult it is to establish a new turning point and to rebuild an environment that can have an impact!

We must understand that there is a period of internal struggle that cannot be revealed until a certain standard is established through which we can have an impact throughout history. When we have a foundation that can influence the leaders of the nation, it will be possible to innovate the entire nation into a new realm. If the influence is limited to a narrow scope, it may only affect a village, a family, or even an individual.

In terms of the restoration providence, until now, God has presented this innovative movement to the world of evil, but its influence has never directly reached society and the nation. It has always been the case that individuals first receive that influence and then engage in movements to unite families, which has brought history to this point. This is the traditional path that individuals must walk in the process of providential history today.

When we look at the religious world today, which has emerged from individuals to families, clans, tribes, nations, and global standards, we can see that every religion has woven a history of struggle. Such a history has not emerged openly through struggle; rather, it has developed while concealing oneself, being cornered by the environment, or failing to utilize progressive factors in a constrained environment while maintaining a public posture.

When we think of this fact, the position of a providential leader who bears responsibility is never a free one. It is not a position where one can reveal oneself, assert oneself, or act recklessly.

One must conceal all the conditions of their original actions and present more beneficial conditions than the current social environment to those they encounter in the new social environment. They must establish relationships with those people and stand in a position where they can connect their true identity and develop.

This is the historical path of the restoration providence.

When we reflect on the historical ancestors of the past, we see that they were always in the position of a messenger, meaning they could not reveal their true identity and had to conceal it. We must understand that these people worked tirelessly to carve out their foothold in such environments.

From this perspective, today, in front of the stage where Satan occupies this world and has numerous sovereign nations, God's restoration providence and salvation providence aim to overturn this nation and the world entirely. Therefore, whenever a manifestation of this providence appears, it stands in a position that cannot be opposed by any nation or society. Thus, those who enter a position of opposition, in other words, those who take responsibility for the providence, always have the heart of a messenger. Such a person has carried out the mission of a messenger sent to the enemy's nation, meaning they have taken responsibility for the sovereignty of that nation and have been determining the fate that can lead to that sovereignty.

For this reason, Christianity entering Rome also went through such a historical process. When the actions of individual messengers are presented in the family, tribal, and national scope, this becomes a new beacon of revolution in that society, allowing for the establishment of a new nation. This is an undeniable fact. From this perspective, we can see that in order for religion itself to develop until now, the responsibility of messengers behind the scenes has been immense. Those who left behind a heavenly lineage to fulfill the mission of a messenger sent to the enemy's nation were those who fulfilled their responsibilities before Heaven in that era, while those who could not do so did not fulfill their responsibilities before Heaven.

**The Hardships of the Messenger**

Our Unification Church has also walked a similar path of destiny while bearing the overall responsibility of God's restoration providence. Moreover, the teacher who presented that responsibility and took on the whole also walked a similar path. Although I was born on the foundation of the Republic of Korea and as part of the same Korean ethnicity, I could not start from a position of trust within this nation and this ethnicity. Truly, I have carried out social activities while concealing all my inner circumstances in a lonely position.

If one cannot overcome the difficult environment that Heaven has set up and developed, they cannot fulfill the great responsibility that determines the fate of the homeland. Therefore, whenever we look at the great mission for the homeland, the attitude and actions of the individual bearing the mission of a messenger must be serious.

For example, North Korea is sending spies to South Korea. In order for these spies to be sent, they must first undergo training to live as spies. So, what must they acquire first during their training? They must learn all the customs of South Korea. They must speak in the South Korean dialect and also learn the lifestyle of South Korea. Their fate of life and death depends on how well they adapt to the life of South Korea.

Therefore, how to make oneself absorbable in every professional field from the living environment is the principle of spy training. There must not be any aspect that seems awkward or strange to those who have lived in South Korea, whether in speech or lifestyle. They must express and live out the ordinary and universal environment as it is in their lives.

In North Korea, there are customs of North Korean people, lifestyles of North Korean people, and social systems unique to North Korea, which can unconsciously manifest in any environment. Yet, to remove all of this and act as a person from another country or region is incredibly difficult. It requires double or triple the effort. We can infer that spies must think twice or three times and act carefully in every action or even in every word they speak.

If their behavior or speech differs even slightly from others, or if their lifestyle is somewhat different, it can become a clue that reveals their true identity. Thus, living in a place different from the environment they have lived in is the life of a spy. To live such a life, how great must the inner hardships be? And how much training must they undergo to become accustomed to such a life? We are also living this kind of life.

Today, the leaders of our Unification Church in the regions are now in a slightly better position, but in the early days, they had to live in a position akin to that of a spy or a messenger on a special mission. So, what must they do to live such a life? They must not adopt an attitude of asserting themselves and trying to apply it to the entire region.

However, when we consider all the past history that the leaders of our Unification Church have walked through until now, we find that they have not lived in such a way. Upon arriving in the region, they immediately revealed everything in their hearts according to their own beliefs, regardless of how those around them might think, and spoke from a position of solo dominance. We cannot help but recall that such actions have caused significant obstacles to our activities.

Having paid all the costs of sacrifice in such an environment, we have now reached a foundation that can be recognized by the leaders of the Republic of Korea. Until reaching this foundation, you may have come from a position of irresponsibility, but the teacher who bears the overall responsibility has faced immense hardships and struggles, which you must understand. While you can act freely in the regions, the teacher who is responsible for the whole has been fighting within the boundaries of a life that has not yet surpassed the standards of a messenger's mission.

The Path a Missionary Must Take
When you work as the leader of that region, if you wield the authority of a leader and arbitrarily dictate things, you will receive criticism from many people. How do you evade the arrows of such criticism? This is the most significant issue that any leader in any position must first transcend. Even at that moment, one must fulfill the missionary's mission. In other words, at that time, one must bury one's identity and not reveal it.

Therefore, even if one feels unpleasant in the environment one is involved in, one must not give an unpleasant impression to the other party. That person may become an enemy at any time. You must become close to those who could become enemies.
The issue is not money. Can you exchange money for my life? No matter what you give, it cannot be exchanged for life. We must build a fence to protect life. 

To do this, one must not sit comfortably and have others run errands for them while they are elevated. The mission of a messenger itself is important. The question is whether you can show a central attitude before them, having fully adapted to that environment with a hundred percent of your original lifestyle and more. To do so, you must not eat better than others. You must not dress better than others. You must not live better than others. 

Even if you live so well that all the people in the neighborhood envy you, you cannot adapt to that environment based on that. It may connect you to a privileged class, but the whole will not comply with you from the bottom up. The enemy can appear anywhere regardless of whether you want to harm them or not, so you must not be connected only to the privileged class. Because the whole is the enemy, you must stand in a position to adapt to the whole and have a lifestyle that can prepare for defense. 

If you are responsible for a region for two years, you must live that way for two-thirds of that period. Otherwise, you cannot manage that village or environment. When we divide the responsibility into three stages: revival, growth, and completion, during the revival and growth stages, two-thirds must be spent in an unhappy position. 

When you reflect on this issue critically, you must reflect on your lifestyle and ideas from the 1960s until now, knowing your intentions. Or did you come out with the goal of your own success centered on the Unification Church, showing your sense of authority? This is a significant issue. 

Caring for oneself may seem good at first, but it leads to ruin. It is the same in the world. It is the same before general nations or their people. The path a messenger must take is precisely this path.

Also, what can I offer to the leaders of that neighborhood? You must appear with some form that can be beneficial as the closest person to the leaders who are guiding that village. 

Resolve anew according to the new command. 

Today, the Unification Church is paving this path. The people of the neighborhood recognize and discern him. The negative rumors about our Unification Church today did not arise because the teacher made mistakes. It all happened because of traitors. Those who spread rumors about the sacrifices made on the path of a messenger are all traitors. They are those who have joined the ranks of traitors.

Until now, in the process of God's restoration, everything such as heavenly order, etiquette, and manners has been accumulated. 3)
New Record
When we think of competition, it evokes images of a game. Victory must go through the process of determining win or loss in a game. Today, we are walking the path of faith. This is akin to stepping into a stadium aiming for victory and competing. Here, the game does not refer to a physical sport but rather to the competition centered around our daily lives, or our life experiences and the history of our nation.

Faithful like standing in a race
Today’s advanced countries have become so because their entire populations have united and made greater efforts than those of other nations. So why has our Republic of Korea become a developing country? The reason Korea has become a developing country is that the entire populace has neglected their efforts and has not worked hard in the historical process of competing with other countries. Thus, it naturally became a developing country. When we look at this fact, we can see that history and the fate of the world have progressed based on such processes.

Now, stepping away from the broad world and returning to ourselves, we must critically examine where we stand in comparison to others. The question arises: what position am I in right now? In this light, you must understand that you are all in a position of racing toward the restoration of the relationship between God and humanity, in other words, between the Father and me. As Paul said, we are those who stand in a race, running toward a single goal; we too are running toward a single objective.

One of the most important competitions in the world is the marathon. Every nation regards winning and setting new records in the marathon as the highest honor. Why is that? Because the marathon is a race that ordinary people cannot complete. The distance of a marathon is extremely long. To win, one must overcome that long distance. Additionally, while winning in the marathon is important, what is even more important is how to set a new record. Just winning is not enough. Even if one cannot set a record as good as the last competition, they can still win. However, what all nations desire in a marathon is not just victory but how to set a new record.

To set a new record
So how can we break the previous record and set a new one? One must put in more effort than all the athletes who have participated in marathons up to now and overcome difficulties. Anyone who does not think this way cannot break the previous record. Even if they win, they cannot set a new record. Moreover, no matter how hard one tries, if they do not strategize well, they cannot set a new record. To set a new record, one must strategize well. In a marathon, strategizing well means that the runner must know themselves well. They must be aware of their physical condition, which changes according to the time and distance they run. In other words, they must know their physical strength and ability that change over a certain time and distance. They must understand that exceeding a certain level will not allow them to maintain a normal physical condition and must adjust their body according to their physical strength. Without doing so, they cannot set a record.

Furthermore, just because one runs well does not mean they should start out in first place. They must adjust themselves to adapt to the set distance. This is the problem. As they approach the final finish line, how will they maintain their initial speed, and how will they reserve the capacity to break through the final finish line? This is crucial. If they cannot adjust this, they cannot win, and even if they do win, they cannot set a new record.

Victory is decided in an instant. The moment one crosses the finish line is less than a minute, or even less than a second. In such a short time, victory is determined. Even if they have run a hundred miles together, the division between first and second place can be decided within just a meter or so. Indeed, victory can be determined by a difference of ten centimeters, one centimeter, or even half a millimeter. The determination of a new record does not depend on the length of time saved but rather on the fact that even if one saves one second, it is still a new record. Likewise, historical records can be broken even by very short distances. Similarly, this is a matter that arises on the path of restoration we are walking.

The goals of the Unification Church
The central goal of the Unification Church is, of course, world restoration. We are running toward that goal. What are we centered on in our running? Until now, religions, that is, religions before 1960, centered on the individual. However, the Unification Church is running a familial race centered on the purpose of the restoration providence. In other words, the Unification Church has entered into the realm of familial racing. This is the difference between the Unification Church and previous religions.

Looking at the history of providential work until now, we can see that God has labored greatly to find the one lost Adam. But can we set a record of victory just by finding one Adam? No. Who testifies to that? Jesus. Jesus came to this earth and stood in the position of a son of God, ready to take responsibility, but could he establish a new record of victory in the restoration providence just with that? No. No matter how excellent Adam was, he alone could not break the record. Because Jesus came and went, God did not set a new record but rather established a record of failure. A gap of two thousand years was created in the path of restoration providence. Instead of setting a new record as a victor, only a record of defeat was established.

So how can the Unification Church today set a new record? First, we must establish a family centered on one man and one woman through the formula of the restoration providence. Then, we must move toward the goal and achieve victory along with good records. Only then can a new origin be established from there. This origin will become the eternal standard in the new era to come. We are moving forward centered on such a tremendous goal.
After today's training, you will scatter in all directions: east, west, south, and north. Everyone will disperse. There will be no one to cheer you on. Not only will there be no support, but various oppositions and persecutions will arise. From that standpoint, you are standing in the arena. Therefore, you must not forget this awareness. You must remember that you are a runner, a person who must go, and that you must run toward your goal even at this moment.

Even if you all end up scattered in different positions and situations, the one thing you must hold onto without change is the thought that I am a racing person. You are people running centered around a goal. When you run, heaven and earth watch over you and silently cheer you on. You are running in this cosmic arena. You cannot run alone; you should not run solely as an individual.

However, until now, this kind of running has continued, but it has not yet become a national competition. It has merely been a small competition that goes back and forth within villages or towns. Such competitions have no relation to provincial or national competitions. No matter how many records you set in village or town competitions, they have no connection to national competitions. Even if you have run, it is limited to that village or town. Those competitions have not been observed by the citizens of the province or the nation.

Thus, having only new records from competitions centered around a single church or school is not sufficient. Only by competing and winning in national or even world competitions can those records become world records.

So, what kind of competition is the Unification Church proposing today? This competition is an enormous one among competitions. It mobilizes ancestors who have come and gone in the past, the current humanity, and countless descendants who will come in the future. In this focal point where three eras are united and mobilized, you are currently running. The issue here is your posture as runners.

What a racer must know
This is where the problem arises for you. Running does not simply mean running unconditionally. You must clearly know your destination. You need to understand where that goal is and how far away it is. No matter how good your posture is, if you do not know the course you need to run, you cannot reach your destination. The course is based on the principle of return, so you must run centered around that.

There are about 70 people here, and not everyone can be first in their running. Among you, there will only be one winner. The question of who comes in first is important. Then what does God desire? God does not look for second place; He looks for first place. He does not look at the many people but focuses on one person. So, when that individual does their best to run, heaven and earth become one.

The issue arises depending on how far that distance is. Until today, human beings have wished and worked day and night for that one day centered around the restoration providence, but the important question is based on what standard they have wished and worked. To restore a nation, individuals must first be restored, and then families, tribes, nations, and countries must be restored. As the scope increases according to each stage, the level of interest in it also rises. You must understand that.

For example, even if an athlete representing a county has an excellent record, they cannot be recognized in front of an athlete representing a province. No matter how good their record is, to be recognized by the provincial athlete, they must compete again and win. Furthermore, even if the provincial athlete's record is significantly better than the national athlete's record, if that record is not from a nationally recognized competition, they cannot be called a record holder of South Korea. However, if in a national competition, even if they fall a few seconds short of their own record, if they break the national standard record, they will achieve the glory of setting a new record. The same applies to breaking world records. Even if a new world record is set within South Korea, it will not be recognized unless it is achieved in a global competition.

Until now, even if you have run well individually, the stage has now widened, and you must run on this broader stage. Running as a representative of a town is different from running as a representative of a county. Running in a county is different from running in a province, and running in a province is different from running for the country. You must be aware of this timing. You must realize that you are a runner who has taken responsibility centered around that time. In running, both the timing and the environment change. Therefore, you must harmonize the changed environment with your own abilities and accept the various phenomena that arise along the way. There is a possibility that enemies may appear.

In running, who is cheering for you? No one is. However, the absence of supporters is not a problem. Enemies will do everything they can to trip you up, and this is the issue. There may be those hiding in unseen corners shooting arrows, or those climbing walls trying to trip you. There will be all sorts of people. In such harsh environments, you must face it and not be invaded. You must have the mindset that if you stumble over an enemy, it will be a serious problem, and you must be able to defend yourself in preparation for the difficult environment. Supporters only watch their own side.

Setting new records on a global stage
From this perspective, today we have raised the banner of world restoration. So, what is the biggest issue for you who have entered the era of world restoration? To restore the world, you cannot rely on records set individually as before. Records set tribally are also insufficient, and records set nationally will not suffice. You must become someone who can appear on the world stage and set new records.

God has been conducting the restoration providence from the highest standard until now. If you do not stand in the position of breaking the records of the satanic world, God's authority, prestige, and face in restoring humanity will not stand. This is God's position. Therefore, our mission, which comes first, is to subjugate everything in the satanic world on the path of restoration and to return the highest glory and authority to God, establishing it. That is why we have stepped onto the global stage.

Then, does that mean that all the people of the country and every family must step forward? No. For a nation, it is sufficient to present just one person as a representative. You only need to send one person who can set a new record.

In the providential process today, you must center around your family and create the origin of a new family to start a new life. Without a new life starting, new ideals cannot begin, and new love cannot emerge. Based on this standard, you must know where that starting point should be. Just having victory here is not enough. If that victory is a victory that is caught by even one thing in the satanic world, you cannot establish God's authority and face to make a new start. This victory must be historical.

We are currently running on a family level. In running, you must run based on numerous connections related to the providential will of heaven and earth, centered on God's heart. Even if you stumble during the race, you must enter the final finish line ahead, even if it is just by one step. It is not just about being ahead; you must be ahead enough to set a new record. This is the path of the restoration providence.

Is the path you are running on centered around one year? No. If it cannot be done in one generation, it must be done in the second generation; if not in the second generation, it must be done in the third generation. Therefore, the restoration providence has been running through the three generations of Adam, Jesus, and the Lord of the Second Advent. It has also passed through the three generations of the God of Abraham, the God of Isaac, and the God of Jacob.

So, how many generations are we in now? We are in the last third generation. If we are in the last third generation, how much of the finish line remains? Have we passed one-third, or have we passed four-fifths? You must know this clearly. And you must mobilize all your latent power and strength to run toward the final finish line.

He must invest all of himself day and night into this. This must not be done from a position of receiving orders or being forced; it must be done voluntarily. Only then can hope sprout, conditions for happiness be presented, and thus, the determination of success or failure be made.

We must understand that Jesus Christ was in a position to invest his entire life and even sacrifice his life to fulfill his responsibility with a heart that loves all humanity. When he stands in a position to face God or humanity, Jesus reigns as God's heir.
will be established. Furthermore, concerning descendants, one must be in a position to inherit their professional field, meaning one must establish a successor.

To inherit God's professional field
To inherit the true and professional field of God, one must be in a true position. One must put forth sincere effort to meet relative standards. The same applies to the effort made to achieve that purpose. One must stand in a position that is worthy of inheritance. Thus, when one stands before God as a professional, God recognizes them as His representative.

To stand in such a position, just as God knows us, we must also strive to know God. Just as God is resolved around the responsibilities He must fulfill in the future, we too must make resolutions. Furthermore, just as God's desired purpose is thorough, our purpose must also be thorough. Although the historical background and the environmental context may differ, one must accompany history centered on that will and stand in a central position representing the era, so that God can joyfully grant the entirety to that person.

In this position, how does Jesus differ from God? God is in an internal position, while Jesus is in an external position. In other words, God is in a subjective position, while Jesus is in an objective position. Furthermore, God stands in a vertical position, while Jesus stands in a horizontal position. Although the positions they stand in are different, in the professional field, they are united with the motivation and all conditions to become one; this is the relationship between God and Jesus.

Therefore, if God is the internal Father, then Jesus is the external Father. When the connection of this internal and external Father becomes one, the previously separated heaven and earth can be integrated. Of course, the subjective role that can unify this is carried out by God, who is in the internal position, but the decision-making from the external position must be done by Jesus. Thus, the expert Jesus, who bears the historical responsibility of restoration, must have successors like his disciples or sons.

Jesus, who could not find a successor
When considering the professional field, Jesus is a global individual among individuals. Among families, the family in which Jesus was born is a global family. There are many tribes, but among them, the tribe that can host Jesus is a historical tribe. Furthermore, if there is a nation that Jesus pursues through the providential course, that nation stands in a position more valuable than any other nation of its time. The world He seeks must also be the highest world.

For this reason, when looking at the professional field of restoration providence, no matter who in any era came forth with the will of providence and bore a historical mission, they must stand in a more professional position than that person. For Jesus, who stands in such a position, to have disciples who can stand in the position of the object He desires, they must be the best among disciples, and to be a son, they must be the best among sons. They must be a chief disciple who can relate to all matters leading up to their professional field. Jesus must grant all His inheritance to such a person. In other words, whether it is an internal emotional issue or an external family issue, or a hope in the course of restoration, there was a need for a successor in the professional field who could fully inherit this.

From this perspective, when Jesus represented the Israelite people and faced the world, He appeared as the highest authority on the path of restoration, but the question of who could inherit His position became an issue. Therefore, Jesus could not help but think about who could stand in such a position among the people of Israel. To find such a successor, Jesus had to take practical actions in all aspects of life. However, when there was no representative standard around Him, He had to travel the country to find a suitable person.

In this way, to establish a successor who could inherit all of Jesus' things, God wove together 4,000 years of history. Nevertheless, the fact that there was no such successor became a sorrow for God and a historical sorrow. It also became a sorrow for Jesus and a global sorrow.

Through 4,000 years of history, God walked the path of suffering while hoping that the chosen people of Israel would become a global foundation that could inherit Jesus' will. However, those chosen people of Israel found themselves in a position where they could not have hope before the expert Jesus. Thus, although Jesus stood in a position of authority as an expert, there was no counterpart to face Him, so this had to be newly sought on earth. Therefore, He had to stand in a position where they needed to be re-educated. This is the path of public life that Jesus had to walk.

So, how should He cultivate successors through this path? From the very beginning, Jesus could not be in a position to teach about His professional field, so He had to become an expert who could do so directly. And the question was how quickly He could pass on that historical task.

Jesus had to prepare the fastest path to inherit not only matters in His professional field but also issues outside of it. This was Jesus' position.

If this cannot be done this year, it can be done next year, or if it cannot be done in the 20s, it can be extended to the 30s, and if not in the 30s, then to the 40s. If it could be done throughout one's life, there would be no problem, but how anxious must Jesus have felt, being in a position where He had to inherit this within a limited period?

As we have learned through principles, there must be conditions and a period, and a central being to replace Adam is needed. In the course of restoration providence, these three essential conditions are necessary. So, who becomes a conditional being before Jesus? Can they appear as a conditional entity based on the resolved conditional period? How do this conditional being and the Adamic being, Jesus, unite? We know that these issues of restoration providence must be determined based on the content of indemnity. This is the expectation of faith and the expectation of substance.

Jesus' sorrowful heart
Then, how do we align the Abel-like being and the conditions that appear before that Abel-like being? For that alignment to occur, the subject and object, which are internal and external relationships, must be in harmony. If that alignment does not occur, the providence of salvation, such as inheritance and indemnity, cannot be fulfilled. So, who is the conditional being that can indeed align with Jesus, who bears the universal responsibility? There was none. Because there was none, they had to be raised. Thus, the path Jesus had to walk was long, and the hope He desired was great, yet because there was no such figure, He had to deal with ignorant fishermen. We must understand how lonely and sorrowful Jesus' plight was.

What was the mission that Jesus had to teach during His three years of public life? It was to teach about God. Since Jesus inherited everything from God, He had to teach about God centered on that traditional content. Next, He had to teach about Himself, and then He had to teach His disciples what kind of beings they were. From this perspective, could Jesus truly teach about God? Could He also teach about Himself? Throughout His three years of public life, He could not teach the entirety of God, nor could He teach the entirety of Himself, nor could He teach all His twelve disciples, including Peter and James.

In this light, how great must have been the loneliness of Jesus, who knew the time he had to fulfill his providential responsibility as an expert, yet lacked the existence of a being who could inherit that.

"If I have told you earthly things and you do not believe, how can you believe if I tell you heavenly things?" (John 3:12), "I still have many things to say to you, but you cannot bear them now." (John 16:12). Based on these biblical passages, we see that Jesus, as an authoritative expert, had to connect the earthly and heavenly, yet how miserable He must have felt without the relative conditions and successors to do so.

Let’s assume you made a world-class invention in some professional field. This fact, known only to you, must be revealed to the world due to a heavenly connection and heavenly mandate. For this reason, Jesus struggled to resolve this during His public life. However, He went the way of the cross without reaching a day of fulfillment of His wishes.

is not alone in starting any action. There must be something that enables the action to take place. There must be a relative relationship. To create this relative relationship, there must be a subject and an object, and this subject and object must have some decisive factors for establishing a relationship. Without this, a relative relationship cannot be formed.

All actions require a relative relationship. Even in the solar system, the sun itself holds a subjective position, allowing the celestial bodies in a relative position to act. Similarly, all existing entities must have a basis that can determine the criteria for the subject and object; otherwise, order or organization cannot be established. Once the subject is determined and the object is defined, all order and organization arise. We understand that today’s phenomena and the world of all things are structured in this way. Nature operates under such principles.

The human body moves and maintains life centered around the heart. When we consider our minds, there is also a center in the mind. This center is absolute in human relationships. It is the personality that humans possess. Based on this personality, humans have lived their lives up to now.

So, what defines a person as a personality? A person who can stand in a central position within a society's system is referred to as a personality. For example, if there is a respected personality in a neighborhood, that person can have a central role in the lives of those living inside and outside that neighborhood, both practically and mentally. Only then can they become an object of respect.

The same is true for a nation. A nation is formed around a representative, that is, a personality. The people form a substantial organization by establishing a relative relationship centered on that personality. When we think about this, there must also be a central personality in the broader world.

Even if we call someone a personality, externally, that person may not differ much from an ordinary person. However, internally, their ideological or mental aspects differ from those of ordinary people.

From this perspective, we can see that what determines a personality is not the external aspect of a person but rather the mental aspect. Therefore, we must discuss personality based on the mental domain of humans.

To become one who expands this mental domain, one must understand the world of the heart. The heart possesses the ability to engage infinitely. In this regard, we can understand that human desires do not arise from the body but from the heart. The heart endlessly acts and generates infinite desires.

When we focus on our personality, we see that personality is not limited to any social, national, or worldly boundaries. Furthermore, it is moving forward while looking at the absolute highest standards that can transcend the past, present, and future. When we observe the inner workings that seek to reach such an absolute position, we can see that the world of the heart is connected to the infinite.

However, the question remains whether this heart is established as an absolute standard in the mental world. This has been a problem until now. When the heart occupies such a position, it establishes the point at which humans can become the masters. What kind of position would that be? It is a central position where the requirements for the highest happiness and absolute values can be determined. However, even if one stands in such a position, there will be the highest existence visible, the highest value, and the highest treasure. What is the standard of personality that can become an absolute center? It cannot be reached with a personality centered only on individual humans. That is why we seek God or the absolute.
