In other words, one should not desire to become one externally in a relative relationship but should seek to become one internally.

Our hearts seek the absolute highest standards. Therefore, if God exists, we would want to become one centered on that God. God desires not an external unity but a unity that can connect to the highest values of internal standards.

When parents want to become one with their children, they do not seek unity in daily life but in the world of the heart, that is, in the world of love. Similarly, when a person wishes to become one with the absolute, it is because they want to stand in a central position.

According to the principle, within the subject, there are internal and external aspects, essence and form, and relationships of superiority and inferiority. To present the idea of unity and a common purpose, the subject must have relationships of superiority and inferiority and relationships of before and after. Such a conclusion arises when we consider the human heart.

All beings, including humans, operate in a 360-degree manner, changing direction based on the subject. However, in a position where the direction of the subject's movement and the environment it is in change, one cannot feel fixed and infinite happiness. So where can one obtain eternal happiness? It is in a position that has absolute authority with content that is unified with the subject. That position is one that governs and directs all things. Only when one is in such a position do the conditions for happiness arise.

A person feels happiness when they become the center of all things and can govern those things as they establish relative conditions. Therefore, humans must determine their central position in front of an absolute standard that mobilizes the relationships of the absolute being of the universe and the relationships of superiority and inferiority. Without doing so, one cannot feel the highest happiness.

So how should such a relationship be established? It should be established based on the love of a parent-child relationship. The relationship centered on love between a parent and child is a vertical relationship, while the relationship between husband and wife is a horizontal relationship. Thus, in Korea, there is a saying that one trusts their children more than their spouse. This reflects the importance placed on the relationship of superiority and inferiority.

What humans fundamentally pursue is to enter the position of the absolute and become one with the subject from that position. When one enters such a position, a relationship of superiority and inferiority is formed. When a relative relationship is formed here, it becomes a horizontal relationship of plus and minus, that is, the subject...
And the relative relationship with the object is established. This is precisely what we call the love between husband and wife for us humans. 

The greatest issue for humans is the pursuit of the ultimate center, that is, becoming one with the Absolute Being. In the pursuit of the nouns 'Absolute' and 'Relative', humans must transcend relative standards and become one with the Absolute Being. Only then can the relationship of higher and lower be established. Humans must enter into this position of hierarchy. Thus, they must become one with the Absolute Being, the origin of all existence, and possess absolute content. When standing in a position of oneness with the Absolute Being, his happiness can become my happiness, his ideals can become my ideals, his circumstances can become my circumstances, and all his relationships and connections can become my relationships and connections. In this way, a complete relationship of husband and wife is formed. Humans are originally meant to start from such a position.

When the human, the center of harmony, becomes one with the Absolute Being, humans are the center of harmony. However, for harmony to occur, an absolute central standard must be established. Just as various people must connect well in a hierarchy centered around a conductor to keep time, the center of harmony in this universe is human, as we have learned through principles. Because such a human is in a position aligned with absolute standards, where that human resides, the universe resides, and the world of existence acts centered around him. And as a result of that action, power arises in the world of existence.

What has God been lamenting until now? God is a spiritual being, like the mind. Such a God wishes to become one with a being like the body. This being like the body is precisely humans. Therefore, humans must become one with God, who is a being like the mind. However, they are not able to become one. This is precisely the reason why God has been lamenting until now. When humans become one with God, the universe will automatically become one. Why does it become one automatically? The universe, created by God, takes humans as the subject and stands in the position of the object. In that position, they must become one with humans. Only then can relationships be established within the realm of creation. When humans become one with God, all beings can also establish relationships with God and humans. The relationship here is not one of opposing positions but rather a relationship that can be given and received from a relative standpoint. The scope of that relationship is super-cosmic. Thus, the relative relationship centered on the Absolute Being is connected even to the realm of absolute authority, so there cannot be any existence that escapes that realm. Therefore, when humans, who can connect the Absolute Being and all things, become one with the Absolute Being, the universe naturally unifies.

If a representative personal center desired by humans had been determined in the historical age, the world of harmony would have undoubtedly emerged. When the center is determined, harmony must occur. As our principles state, a perfect center creates a perfect relative. All existing things cannot exist beyond relative factors, so there must be a subject and an object in existence. In other words, if there is a perfect subject, there is a relative. All existence possesses the attributes of God and exists within the universe, thus existing relatively according to the principles of creation.

Humans have pursued a centered personality through the 6,000 years of historical process. Countless ancestors have walked the path of effort to find this. Humans have sought a personality that can adapt to their environment and an ideal world centered around that personality through many eras. Humans must give and receive with the relative to become a whole. A person of character must be able to dominate the relative. That relative can be a nation or a homeland. Therefore, a global person of character must have a global citizenry and a global homeland. From this perspective, God Himself must also have a cosmic people. God is the same. The union of heaven and earth is referred to as the "Heavenly Nation" in the Unification Church. The one who can be the master here is the "Heavenly People." And the foundation on which these Heavenly People can stand is the land of the Kingdom of Heaven. God must also have such a foundation.

Then, when a person enters the absolute position and stands in the subjective position, will they become a person who desires nothing? No, that is not the case. When one stands in the absolute position, they will inevitably pursue a second desire. That is the pursuit of the relative.

Humans must approach the absolute position. After that, they must establish a relationship with the relative centered on the absolute subject. The larger the scope, the closer they can stand to the realm of absolute authority. Therefore, if one is in a position to govern a nation, they must enter closer to the realm of absolute authority centered on that nation.

Transcending the historical age, if one becomes a representative leader before the nation, they will undoubtedly enter the global realm. The more one enters this global realm, the broader the scope becomes. In this way, the desire to create one's world centered on the absolute authority arises. From this perspective, humans cannot be happy as the absolute standard itself. Relative conditions are inevitably necessary. Likewise, God must determine the standard of relative personality and have a relative world centered on that personality. Without this, happiness cannot be attained. When one becomes a person who can turn happiness toward God, that person becomes the standard in the historical age.

The highest position humans pursue
Throughout the 6,000 years of historical process, we humans have hoped for and pursued an absolute purpose, absolute existence, and absolute love centered on God. However, we have not been able to stand in a position that can connect such purpose, existence, and love. Although we have traversed historical distances, to become such an existence in this era, we must receive recognition from the Absolute Being. This is the problem. Until now, there has been only one such person: Jesus.

Jesus said, "God is my Father." There is no clearer statement that represents the relationship between the absolute being and oneself. And among all the statements that refer to relative relationships, there can be no better statement than "I am the subject, and you are the objects. I am the bridegroom, and you are the brides." Therefore, this relationship must be connected to all humanity in reality. In connecting, it is not about connecting based on material values. It is not about connecting centered on the current physical human. So what should we center our connection on? We must connect centered on love.

No matter how much we establish the absolute existence or the absolute purpose, if we are not joyful there, it is of no use. Living and thriving should be joyful. Living is for the purpose of achieving goals. When that goal is achieved, there will be something new beyond existence itself.

What is that? When viewed from the perspective of men and women, what is the most precious thing for them? It is love. Only love can become the factor of happiness that connects this. No matter how well a person sets a goal, if they cannot establish the authority of subjective love to govern that goal, they will have to pursue a new goal again. The limit of a goal cannot be above love.

Then, has there been anyone in the historical age who has confirmed the Absolute Being and the love of the Absolute Being? The only person who can say that such a standard has been established is Jesus. How did Jesus confirm the relationship with the Absolute Being? He confirmed it by calling God his Father.

What is Jesus' purpose? It is to establish the world of goodness. It is to create a new world of goodness desired by the Father and the Son. That world is a relative world that can only be realized when the Father and the Son are absolutely connected. If there is no absolute connection between the Father and the Son, that world cannot be expected. The Father must have a Son. What position does that Son occupy? It is the position confirmed as the relative existence of the Absolute Being, capable of being God's counterpart.

Then, what do the Father and the Son commonly require? They require a world where both become an absolute entity and can communicate with each other through that absolute relationship. Any world outside of that is a false world. To establish a relationship with such a world, it cannot be done with means and methods. It cannot be done with money. Love must be present. A structure must be established centered on love, and order must be established.

If there is a person who lives for the common purpose of humanity, that person will unite centered on human love. Likewise, if the citizens have patriotism, they will unite centered on the spirit of patriotism. The stronger the patriotic heart, the more they will unite vertically centered on the spirit of patriotism to form a nation. If one understands that they cannot carry out a patriotic movement alone, they must connect horizontal relationships. This is what gathering comrades means.

The gathering of comrades for the March 1st Movement was for the happiness of the entire nation seeking to find the country. Our nation, which could not find its country, is a pitiful nation. Therefore, to be happy, the whole must unite from the standpoint of loving the country to find the nation. We must seek a beloved country. To be happy, a family must seek a beloved family, and to be happy, the world must seek a beloved world.

From this perspective, what did Jesus Christ proclaim when he came to this earth? What can be the eternal hope that can connect the world as one? It is love. We must understand that where there is no love, there is no hope, no purpose, and no happiness.

We must understand the view of personality presented by Jesus Christ, that is, we humans are the representatives of the Absolute Being. Therefore, as the representatives of the Absolute Being, we must possess absolute love and eternal subjectivity. No matter what hardships come, we must carry this subjectivity. This is the thought of the Messiah. The world Jesus envisioned was an absolute world. Therefore, the world we desire must also be eternal. To realize such a world, we must love. What kind of love must we have? We must love even our enemies, not hate them. This love cannot exclude the entire universe.

Jesus stood in a position where he had to embody such love on behalf of the historical age. Therefore, all humanity must unite to enter this realm. To do this, we must determine a center in any era. Here, the subject who can become the center of harmony is the issue.

**Father and Son**

If God created all things on this earth solely for Himself, then such a God cannot be happy. Furthermore, if God wished to keep all created things as His own forever, He cannot be happy either.

**The Purpose of God's Creation of All Things**

If you have made something with great care, your heart should be more about giving it to someone based on environmental connections rather than wanting to keep it for yourself. The significance lies in making it for someone else.

So, when you make something with care for someone, who is that someone? When you make it for a loved one, you want to create something that exceeds the value of that love and wish to give something beyond that value. It is from such a heart that we feel happiness when we create.

From this perspective, we can see that God did not create the universe with the heart of wanting to serve Himself, but rather with the heart of wanting to give to someone He loves. Therefore, when God created the universe, who was it for? It was for His beloved sons and daughters.

That is why, as the Creator of all things, what position would God want to place humans in? It must be the position of sons and daughters. The heart of a parent is to want to give everything to their beloved sons and daughters, along with their love.

When loved ones exchange a small handkerchief, it is not the handkerchief itself that is precious, but the love conveyed through it that is valuable. Because the love connected to that handkerchief represents overall value, it possesses infinite worth.

Similarly, no matter how joyfully God created this universe, if He cannot give it to someone He loves, then God is in a pitiful position. Therefore, God desires to establish His beloved children and give them all created things along with His entire life and love.

**Humans Who Have Not Inherited Everything from God**

When we consider that there was a time when God could treat humans in this way, we must ask ourselves whether we, as humans, have truly received the things that God has painstakingly created for us. Have we achieved the standard of being the substantial beings that can represent God's dignity? Have we received the love that God wished to give us? When we look at these issues, we see that today’s fallen humanity has not received any of these three things. In other words, we humans have not inherited the created world that God has made.

God created humans as the center of the created world, wishing for them to become a complete man and a complete woman beyond the standard of completion that He desired. He wanted to establish them as relative beings before each other while simultaneously wanting to attach His eternal love that cannot be severed. However, humans have not received any of this.

Because this has become a grievance, humans must establish conditions of restoration to recover it. Since we are humans who have not received all things, we must establish material conditions as sacrificial offerings to recover them.

Next, we must establish personal conditions. Because Adam fell and did not completely inherit the created world from God, a being to replace Adam must emerge. However, this cannot be inherited without conditions of restoration. Therefore, we must understand that Jesus came to be the sacrificial offering representing humanity.

Furthermore, because our human ancestors did not receive God's love, the one who comes as the True Parents on this earth must also offer sacrifices to receive God's love. We must recognize that such responsibilities remain.

We must inherit all things, inherit the substance, and possess relative personalities to inherit God's love, yet we have not received any of these. We must understand that our sorrow and grievance lie in not having inherited all of this.

**In Order to Seek the Position of Inheritance**

We must inevitably inherit all of this. To do so, we must find a position where we can inherit it. We must seek the place where God wants to joyfully give and attach His love. Without finding that place, we cannot inherit.

To find that place, what must we do? If that place is a joyful one, we must approach it with a joyful heart; if it is a sorrowful place, we must approach it with a sorrowful attitude. Without doing so, we cannot find that place. God wanted to give joyfully, but because there was no one to receive it, that place became a place of sorrow. Therefore, to regain it, we must present conditions of joy that exceed the sorrow we have caused God. Otherwise, we will not be qualified to receive.

God's heart is to give to the children who love all things while boasting of the value of life. However, because we lost that position, the division of all things had to occur.

The substance that inherits all things becomes the center of the universe. Additionally, before the subject, the male, the female as his object is also given. Thus, the place where they give and receive is the highest place of joy, and it is a place where not only the couple but all things rejoice. However, we humans have lost this place.

Therefore, today, we humans are in a position where we cannot receive without experiencing sorrow proportional to the joy we could feel in that place. This is the sorrowful path of restoration that we must recognize. Furthermore, we are in a position where we must receive God's love in a place of infinite sorrow, even though we should receive it in a place of infinite joy. We have lost the connection to establish relationships while receiving joy in a joyful place. However, you must understand that to find that place, you must approach it from the opposite perspective. That is why, throughout the long historical process, many sacrificial offerings have appeared before humanity in each era. You must understand that those offerings were tragically sacrificed.

So, what must a person who offers a sacrifice do to become one with the offering? It does not happen just by being in the position of offering. You must understand this. One must be completely united not only in the position of offering but also in the position where the offering grows and dies. Without feeling the pain of the offering and the agony of death as one's own suffering, one cannot become one with the offering. Unless one stands in the position of feeling all the pain that the offering experiences, the condition of having suffered as an offering cannot be established. The place where one is offered as a victorious offering before God is the place of the offering.

**The Hurdles Faithful Must Overcome**

The same applies when we look at Jesus and humanity. Jesus became the offering for humanity on this earth. Therefore, whether we today receive salvation centered on the sacrificial Jesus depends on whether we can experience the entire course up to the point of Jesus becoming the offering. Depending on whether we can experience this, the question of whether we can become complete disciples or complete sons and daughters of faith is determined. In other words, those who only accept Jesus' pain as His pain, standing in a separated position that has no relation to themselves, cannot be in the position of having become an offering and therefore cannot receive complete salvation. Only those who feel the pain of the sacrificial Jesus as their own pain and stand in the position of being one with the offering can receive salvation.

Furthermore, when we think of God's pain from having His love violated, we must experience that pain and that heart of love in order to be restored centered on God's love. We must recognize this connection.

However, when we look at the countless Christian believers who have lived their faith centered on Jesus until now, we must ask whether they have truly experienced the sorrow of Jesus, who was born in sorrow and walked the path of the cross. How great must have been the pain of His heart, who shed blood on the cross for all humanity, yet had to pray for His enemies without harboring a heart of revenge? If we are to fully receive what Jesus wanted to give us, we must stand in a position that exceeds the pain that Jesus bore. We must do so. If we do not stand in such a position, we cannot become beings capable of receiving it.

Because we have not received what Jesus wanted to give us, Jesus has been filled with resentment. So, what is the condition to receive this? It is compassion for the one who is filled with resentment. Without establishing such a connection, we cannot receive.

Now, when we consider the death of Jesus, for whom did He die? He died for all humanity. Today, He died for ourselves.

So, what was the motive for Him to die for us? It is because we stand in a position that cannot be accepted before the heavenly principles, having woven a history of betrayal. Therefore, He died in our place. Should we not sympathize with the pain of the one who died in our place? So, where can we sympathize after overcoming our sins, and where can we find a place to be sympathized with after overcoming our sins? Without becoming an offering, the place of victory and joy cannot be before us. This is the hurdle that faithful must overcome, and it is the internal point of unity that those who offer sacrifices must reach.

**We Must Restore the Vertical History Horizontally**

When we look at our blessed families, husbands and wives must become one centered on God's love. The blessing of being a couple is given based on love, which is the greatest thing God can give. When we consider this, what is the position where we can fully receive it as our own? In other words, what is the position where God wanted to give joyfully?

When we think about Adam and Eve having fallen, which prevented them from giving joy, we must create a connection in that family where we can hear that we are better than Adam and Eve, where we can receive compassion and mercy, and where we can reflect on ourselves. Only then can that become the motive to rekindle God's love.

From this perspective, we today must trace the path of restoration while placing the issue of faith before us. We must restore the vertical history horizontally. We must restore the 6,000 years of history at once from a single point in time. Today, we must horizontally restore the vertical history that has continued through three stages: the age of resurrection for 2,000 years, the age of growth for 2,000 years, and the age of completion for 2,000 years. So, how do we restore the vertical history horizontally? This is an important question.

The 6,000 years of history is a history of offering sacrifices centered on God. It has been a history where all things were offered, where sons were offered, and where one's own substance was offered. Because this has been repeated for 6,000 years, the question is how we can bind ourselves and our families in the same position as Adam and the Adam family in relation to our present selves.

Humans must have families. When we look at families, there are parents, children, and possessions. So, what is the substantial entity that can replace the entire vertical history of the Old Testament, New Testament, and Completed Testament? It is all things, children, and parents. In other words, it is parents, children, and their possessions. These are the things needed within the boundaries of the family.

Then, how can we offer a sacrifice that exceeds the total of all the offerings we have made before God throughout history? This is the question. In other words, how can you offer what you currently possess as a total that exceeds all the offerings made before God from the Old Testament until now?
do you think you can offer it to God? You must understand that the value of your offering is not just in the material itself but in the heart and intention behind it. 

You are called to transcend your own desires and possessions, to recognize that everything you have is a gift from God and should be returned to Him. This is the essence of being a true offering. 

As you prepare to leave this place, remember that you are stepping into a new mission. You must carry with you the understanding that you are a representative of God, and your actions should reflect that. 

In doing so, you will not only fulfill your own destiny but also contribute to the restoration of humanity. The path may be difficult, filled with trials and sacrifices, but it is through these challenges that you will grow and become a true child of God. 

Embrace the loneliness that comes with this journey, for it is in that solitude that you will find strength and clarity. Remember, God is with you, guiding you every step of the way. 

As you move forward, let go of the notion of ownership and embrace the concept of stewardship. Everything you possess is not truly yours; it is entrusted to you by God. Use it wisely and generously for the greater good. 

In the end, your true wealth lies not in material possessions but in your relationship with God and your willingness to serve others. This is the legacy you will leave behind, a testament to your faith and commitment to God's purpose. 

So, as you go forth, carry this message in your heart and let it guide your actions. You are not just living for yourself; you are part of a greater plan, a divine mission that transcends time and space. 

May you find joy and fulfillment in your journey, and may your life be a living testament to the love and grace of God.
Will you establish a connection? To do so, you must hunger. You need to understand this. 
During the 40 days of fasting, when Jesus was tempted by Satan, he was tested on the value of material things, the value of himself, and the value of his relationship with God. To be a son of God, one must transcend material things and oneself. In other words, one must completely deny all relative conditions. You must love God alone to pass the principle of restoration. You must think only of God. It was in such a position that the connection between God and Jesus was established. 
Moreover, that position transcended the desperate heart that craved bread when hungry, surpassing the desires that Adam and Eve had when they fell in the Garden of Eden. It is also a position that transcends the heart that was tormented during the time of Adam and Eve's fall. 
Jesus fasted for 40 days in a state of extreme seriousness, with all his nerves on edge, and his whole body and mind under tremendous pressure. How serious must that position have been? What is a piece of bread compared to anything in the world? You would know if you have ever fasted. 
So, when Satan, centered on all these external circumstances, said, "If you are the Son of God, then turn these stones into bread," he was questioning the infinite value and absolute authority that should come with being a son of God. In the face of death and destruction, what is bread, and what is oneself? The issue is how one stands before God. 
From this standpoint, when Satan says, "If you are the Son of God, do this," it is also saying, "If you are the Son of God, do not do that." In other words, when he says, "If you are the Son of God, turn these stones into bread," he is saying, "As the Son of God, do not do that." The test is whether one can refrain from doing it. 
Similarly, what will you do regarding your own value and the value of material things? What will you do with your own being and material possessions that cannot be exchanged for anything in the world, even if you were to give the whole world? 
In the face of hunger, a dime or a piece of bread cannot be exchanged for anything in the world. When praying before the Father while shedding tears over this piece of bread, one should say, "How sorrowful must you have been, Father, as you sought humanity on the path of restoration? This material is in the position of a sacrifice, and as I eat it, I offer my being in the position of a sacrifice. Please accept this body." 
All things exist for humanity, and humanity exists for the Father, right? Therefore, just as I love material things, may the Father also love this body of mine. I must dedicate myself entirely to become the source of strength that the Father desires, to fulfill all His hopes. 
I must be able to say this. 
I must stand in a position where heaven can long for me with a heart that yearns for bread when I am hungry. When I start from a position where I can receive a love greater than the love that Adam and Eve could not receive because they fell in the Garden of Eden, then the story of restoration can finally be established. 
I must seek such a position. That is the path I must take, the critical path. I must stand in a position where God can long for me even more than I long for bread when I am hungry. Without this, restoration cannot happen. 
So, what must I do? I must live for the Father. Was I not a sinner in the past? However, because He is a Father who loves His children, how much pain must He have felt in dealing with this unfilial child? As I wet His painful heart with endless tears and resolve never to be such a son again, the Father’s pain will disappear. 
Without creating a motive to forget all the sins of the past, the hope to re-establish the connection between the Father and the son cannot be fulfilled. This is the same in the human world. 
How will I become a sacrifice? 
When I think about this, I should not be sad that I was born as a descendant of the fallen. I should not be sad that I do not dress well. I should not be sad that I am beaten by enemies. 
The more miserable and overwhelmingly opposing the conditions are, the more they become the starting point for relating to God's tremendous heart as His son. If there are no such sorrows, there can be no relationship with the joy of heaven, and without the path of the cross, there can be no peaceful road as the Prince of Peace. All connections are made through these opposing phenomena. 
Therefore, if you have not been able to offer your whole self as a sacrifice at some point, you must think about how you will pass through the process of offering each part of yourself as a sacrifice. You must go through the path of sacrifice. How will I make my hands a sacrifice? How will I make my feet a sacrifice? How will I make my head a sacrifice? You must think about your intentions until your head hurts, and when you study something, you must think seriously about it with the utmost sincerity. How much has this body been sacrificed for the purpose? How will my beauty become a sacrifice for the purpose? Even if I offer every single part of my personal being, is there not a place where I can offer it all at once? 
If such a place exists, then I must first offer myself as a sacrifice on behalf of all people. When I stand in such a position, a new historical world will be created from here, and a new providential work of God will develop. 
You must understand that this is the path that the Unification Church members who understand the meaning of the providence of restoration must take today, and it is the normal path that the children of heaven must walk. We must recognize how far our living standards and the path that heaven walks are from each other. In other words, we must completely dedicate ourselves before heaven. 
Do not lament that you have nothing in your married life. God, who looks upon that, feels even more sorrowful and pained. 
Who are you unable to live for? It is not because you lack strength or ability, nor is it because you do not make an effort. It is because you live dedicating that strength and effort only for yourself! 
This is the blessing, and this is the infinite value. Because of this, God has compassion for you. 
Without receiving heaven's compassion, you cannot walk the path of restoration. Therefore, starting from March 1970, the question is how you will find a place to receive heaven's compassion in your life. If you cannot find this place, you cannot establish a connection between the Father and the son. You must clearly understand this. 
The path Abel walks 
When the fate of heaven or the fate of a nation comes through such compassion, the people of that nation receive blessings through those who have left behind the connection of compassion. Isn't this a blessing? The same goes for the fate of a nation. If there is someone who can lead the 30 million people of South Korea and receive compassion from heaven greater than that of the 30 million people, that person can save the entire nation. Even if the entire world of 3 billion people were lost, if there is a representative person who receives compassion greater than that for 3 billion people from heaven, then the way for those 3 billion people to be saved will be opened from that point. 
The path of the Messiah and those who bear the responsibility of Adam's mission is a path of effort and responsibility to fulfill such a mission. That is why we are told to walk the path of suffering. God also drives us to the boundary where Abel was killed. 
God made Noah walk the path of suffering for 120 years. Why? To leave behind a precious compassion during Noah's entire life. That is why he was driven to the path of suffering. 
That is why God also made Abraham leave his beloved hometown, Ur of the Chaldeans, and become a wanderer. Yet, before singing of yesterday's happiness, he stood at the most unhappy point today, carrying the remnants of that happiness as heavenly, and fought to pave the way to sing of happiness in alignment with that value. It was in this journey that Abraham was finally determined to be the ancestor of faith. 
The content of compassion was that abundant. 
When he stood in a lonely position crossing borders, he could feel God's loneliness in losing a nation, and when he became a wanderer in a foreign land, he could feel God's sorrow in providence in that foreign land, which is the world of Satan. Isn't that so? 
Then, when God sees His sons and daughters stepping into such a position, will He not place Himself, His honor, and all His ideals on the line and have compassion? When we think of this as God's sense of responsibility as a parent, we must understand that God driving us to the path of suffering is not to ruin us or take everything away from us. It is God's love to solidify the connection of compassion and to inherit the eternal achievements that will come upon that foundation. 
When we think about this, many of our ancestors left behind the path of defeat before God, focusing only on the momentary processes of their lives. However, God looks beyond the momentary historical processes to the history of thousands and tens of thousands of years before and after, preparing for eternal blessings. We must recognize that many of these ancestors betrayed God. 
To receive God's compassion 
So, as descendants of fallen ancestors, how will we create the path of compassion in our journey? Even if I have material possessions, how can I stand in a position where God would want to give me more? To do this, I must invest everything I own and want to serve God's will even if it means going into debt. One who genuinely serves God's will, regardless of means and methods, will never perish. Even if one goes into debt, God will repay that debt. 
From the perspective of one's own being, even if one is struggling to overcome difficulties and is on the verge of collapse, one must remember that God has endured in even more miserable positions than this. Instead, one should strive to comfort and reconcile with that pitiful Father. Also, even in a collapsing position, when one struggles to take even one more step forward, God will manifest there. 
The greater the compassion, the more actions unfold. So, where is the boundary where God can unfold actions and mobilize? When one stands in the position of receiving the utmost compassion while being invaded and sacrificed, God will be bound to that place and work. Moreover, it is from that place that God makes requests. 
The early history of the Unification Church was such a history. Many people opposed it. I was left alone. However, the more people opposed it, the more I thanked God and struggled to comfort Him. Even when Satan tried to invade that position, God raised a victorious history. 
How much compassion can you receive in your life journey? A person who stands in the position of receiving God's compassion beyond their own neighborhood becomes a son of God who can lead that neighborhood. A person who stands in the position of receiving compassion from God, centered on a district or county, cannot help but be revered by all the people of that district or county. 
When looking at South Korea, even if God forgets South Korea, He cannot forget you. Even if He hates the entire 30 million people, He cannot hate you. 
If there is someone who can evoke compassion that says, "Even if I want to curse heaven and earth, I will leave behind compassion on behalf of heaven and earth," and if there is a son who dances and runs, saying he would be willing to be a sacrifice at the last moment, that son would be able to save all of heaven and earth. 
So how will you create such a connection of compassion? To do this, you must traverse the path of the way. While you are alive, if you do not visit every corner and crevice of the area you are responsible for, it will be a regret. If your body is tired and you must rest, you should pray with tears, saying, "Father! I have many places to go and am busy, but I am sorry to have to rest because I am tired." Then, the path of that person will progress day by day. There is no way for Satan to invade the path of such a person. If he does invade, he will have to compensate several times over. 
From this perspective, you must start this work from March of this year as you enter the 1970s. As fallen prodigals who have betrayed our parents, we cannot return without receiving compassion from our parents. Therefore, you must understand that you must take such a path today. You must receive God's compassion. 
God's desire 
So, in what position does God want to give? He wants to give in the position where humanity can be happy. That is God's original desire. If Adam and Eve had not fallen in the Garden of Eden, they would have received the inheritance of the universe in the glorious position where heaven and earth harmonize. Moreover, they would have received all of God's love. 
However, as fallen beings who have severed our connection with God, where must we begin to reconnect with Him? It cannot be from a position of glory. Because Adam and Eve fell and parted from God with tears, we must restore that connection with tears. That position is where we part with tears, and it is also where life and death intersect. Therefore, we must meet at a place where life and death intersect. 
Just as Jesus prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane, sweating blood, we must meet while shedding blood and tears. We must have a heart of repentance and be determined to expose all the sins historically committed, running toward a path of death that exceeds that. Although Adam and Eve died due to their fall, we, their descendants, must have the heart to face a death tenfold or a hundredfold greater than theirs. Only then can we be restored quickly. 
In this sense, when Jesus prayed, "Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as you will," he was determined to welcome death with joy.
If he had become such a son, how would he have prayed? The teacher has thought about this.  
If he had become such a son, would he have been able to pray, "Let this body, which should rightly die, pass by me"? No, he could not.  
The body born for Your will, the body that must go for Your will and die for Your will has come, so what objection could I have? I was born to joyfully embrace this path of death, and I have lived to walk this path of death. Am I not standing here to walk this path? he would have said.  
If he had left behind a connection of God's compassion with such a heart, what would have happened? What would have truly occurred? How would God have felt when facing such a son? He would have been astounded.  
As God looked at that son, He would have said, "Ah, you are a model for Adam of Eden who did not know My will. You, who say Father at the beginning, Father in the middle, and Father at the end, do you not stand in a place where the absolute connection with the realm of the fall has been severed? Therefore, you must not be invaded by the world of Satan."  
If that had happened, could heaven not have dealt with Judas Iscariot and his group? It could have. We can think about that as well. So, you must also carry this attitude forward.  
How earnest must God be in wanting to give His heart to humanity? If there was a distance between the heart He wanted to give before the fall of Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden and the heart He wanted to give after the fall, restoration would not be possible. You must understand this. The heart He wanted to give after the fall has become even stronger than the heart He wanted to give before the fall.  
Isn't it the same for humans? If a child of a wealthy family falls into a position where he cannot inherit due to his unfilial behavior, the parents would feel, "If you had not done this, I could have given you everything..." That feeling surges even more.  
In the future, if a better son than you comes along, the parents would feel even more eager to pass on their inheritance to that son.  
In other words, God wanted to give everything to Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden through a law of autonomy, within the realm of natural law, but because Adam and Eve fell, He developed a desire to give from an even more serious and radiant position. For this reason, God has sought a filial son who can forget thoughts of that unfilial child in the hearts of parents. To receive a son greater than that unfilial child, He has overcome all the trials of the fierce Satan and the opposition to heaven throughout all historical processes. We must understand this fact.  
The correct attitude we must take before the Father  
So how can we become such a son? We must say that even if the conditions are set that would inevitably lead to unfilial behavior, we cannot act unfilially no matter what. Even if we are pushed into such a position a hundred times, we must say we cannot do it. Even if we are pushed ten thousand times, we must still say we cannot do it. No matter how much love or anything else is given to us, we must say we cannot betray the heavenly principles. Even if everything I have is taken away, I must say I cannot do it.  
Then what kind of position can we take? It is the position of believing in God. Even if the treasures of love that I could never have imagined are given to me, I cannot go against the heavenly principles. The position that can do this is the position that denies the fallen Adam and strikes the archangel. Even if everything I love is taken away, I cannot betray the heavenly principles.  
That is the position of God. Even if the entire universe is taken away and all sons and daughters are taken away, the Father cannot be dragged into that.  
How can we internalize the heart of the Father that says, "I cannot do that"? You must internalize this.  
Therefore, even if my beloved parents are taken away, even if my beloved spouse and children are taken away, even if something is taken away from me, I must say I cannot do it. Even if heaven collapses and the universe changes, I must say I was born only for heaven and will die for heaven.  
I must say that I will go regardless of whether heaven acknowledges me or not.  
Fortunately, if heaven acknowledges me, I may die in a place of glory, but even if I become a body that dies in some gutter without heaven's acknowledgment, I will seek that path. If there is a son who can do this, God will bless him. He will want to leave the son's grave in the kingdom of glory, in the garden of Eden. Isn't that the heart of a parent?  
No matter what happens, I must say I cannot betray the heavenly principles. Because the Father came with a destiny that cannot do so, we, as His children, also cannot do so. Isn't that the heart of the Father wanting to give?  
To draw the image of a son who can be loved in front of such a Father, we must strive to find the way of filial piety and the way of loyalty in today's path of restoration. Isn't that the correct attitude we should take? God wants to give from that position.  
What will He give if He gives? He will give everything of the Father. And we will receive everything of the Father. When I try to speak of past sorrows before the Father, He will say, "Hey, stop talking about that. I know all your stories and more. Now let's talk only about the good things that will happen in the future. Do you know how you can stand in the position of My son and how you can serve the Father well?" We must become sons who can hear such words.  
Those who stand in such a position will not perish. As long as heaven remains, he will not perish. If he is thrown into prison and told to die, the one who put him there will rather die. If the nation strikes him, that nation will perish, but he will not perish. If the world strikes him, he will not perish, and rather the world will perish.  
Why is that? It is because his position is the position that represents heaven. Because he represents heaven, he does not perish. If he perishes, the fortune of God and the providence of restoration cannot be fulfilled. Therefore, you must also become such sons and daughters.  
The place where God feels happiness  
The teacher has walked this path and shed blood, but there is still blood left. The teacher still has strength left. The teacher has faced the sorrowful heart of the Father who welcomed the fallen unfilial child and the unfaithful archangel, and how can I resolve the resentment of the Father who lost both the archangel and the filial son at once? I do not mean to stand in the ranks of loyal subjects. If I must die for loyal subjects to come forth, I will die for that.  
You must understand that without the heart that wants to give birth to loyal subjects, you cannot become a son of God. Because the Father has come with the heart of filial piety and loyalty until now, we must also have such a heart. When this happens, God cannot help but show compassion.  
Isn't it human emotion to embrace someone who speaks of their pitiful situation and weep loudly? So, if I step forward to overcome the sorrow of the Father who was saddened by unfilial and unfaithful behavior, will not the Father embrace him and joyfully share all His things?  
If there is someone who has the heart that says, "I cannot even be filial or loyal, but if I can, I will die for the Father," then God will be pleased even in a weary position, or even if the Father comes down to the position of the son and the son goes up to the position of the Father.  
When I say, "I was born for You," the Father says, "I am here for you." You must have the connection where the hearts of the Father and the son can intersect.  
The Father has been leading the providence with the heart to give to us from such a position. Knowing the internal heart of the Father, I must be a son who can be sad before the Father before He is sad, and if there is something that can make the Father happy, I must be the one who can make the Father happy before I am happy. When we stand in such a position, even if God is filled with resentment due to the fall, we must understand that an environment will unfold where He can give when He wants to give.  
When such an environment unfolds where God can give when He wants to give, then He will finally feel happiness. And I will be happy because I can receive what God gives. By establishing a second foundation where humans lost the foundation to give and receive in the Garden of Eden, a new heaven will be connected from here. You must know this and seek the place where you can give and receive. The Father wants to give from such a place.  
To inherit the connection of True Parents  
You must stand in such a position to receive from the Father. Moreover, I should not keep what I receive as my own, but I must give it to my brothers and sisters in the world of Satan, all the Cain-like people, and those in the world of enemies.  
"Father, as You love me and give me joy, I will joyfully give it back to them, so please let this object establish connections of joy wherever it goes." You must be able to do this. This is the way of the gospel and the ideology that our Unification Church must leave behind.  
We must leave this forever. I must leave behind this joy that I received. Until this world is restored and all grievances are resolved, I must leave this for future generations. I must give back the blessings I received in full. Not only what I received from God but also my love must be added to it.  
Then what is the foundation where I can keep what I give? It must become a unified tribe, a unified nation, a unified state, and a unified world. This is the path that our Unification group must take.  
By establishing this, if the sorrow of the Father is completely indemnified, and if the history of humanity, which has been filled with grievances, is indemnified, and if Abel's responsibility is fulfilled, then through me, a point of victory for generations to come will be established. This historical and cosmic responsibility is placed upon our shoulders. In this position, the question is whether we will bear that cross with sorrow or with joy. Will we bear it with joy or with sorrow? We must become sons who can bear the cross with joy, unlike Jesus. We must say we will serve the Father with our lives. Then, we must understand that the Unification Church will absolutely not perish.  
Because the teacher has come this far with such conviction, even if you do not uphold the teacher's will, even if the teacher goes to the spirit world, a foundation will be established on earth to set the connection again. If there is an absolute subject, an absolute object can be created. Because of this law, if we establish the connection of absolute heart on this earth, even if no one believes on this earth, we can create relative conditions that will make the unbelieving world believe.  
You have understood the will. So, if you want to pass on the connection of True Parents centered on the will that the teacher loves, you must have the heart that wants to give everything with the heart of True Parents' love. The day that such a heart departs from you is the day the Unification Church will perish. It will no longer develop.  
However, you must feel the responsibility to invest your life, your wealth, and everything into this. Then the question is how to receive its value and how to leave it for your descendants after receiving it. You must add something precious and attach your love to it. Growing with the flesh of love is the Unification Church and all of you in the Unification Church.  
When you are dying, you must pour all your blood and sweat into this, all your bones and flesh, and even your love, so that even a single point can become flesh and cells, and if you do not grow it and take it with you, you cannot become a people of heaven and cannot have a connection with the heavenly nation. You must clearly understand this.  
The mission of the tribal Messiah  
You must not become a person responsible for receiving. If God has come to receive, this earth will perish. You must resolve the heart of the Father who has longed for a son who can stand before the Father who has come to give.  
When we look at this issue, the question is how we sympathize with those who have sinned. The issue is how we can move to the point of forgetting their sins with a heart that sympathizes with them rather than blaming them for their sins.  
Before pointing out what that woman did wrong or what that man did wrong, if we first establish a heart of compassion, the history of heaven will develop. You must understand this. This is the heart of the Father who deals with humanity, so you must save the pitiful ones with such a heart. This is the mission of a responsible person.  
When saving, you must expend more of your strength than the strength of the person being saved, and you must amplify your wishes more than their wishes. After saving them, you must pass on the fulfillment you felt to the saved person, so that the saved person can also feel the fulfillment of living. This is the mission of the tribal Messiah that you must understand.  
What I want to ask is that wherever you go, please keep in mind that you are the sons and daughters of the Father.  
You must become those who can restore the fallen son who lost the position of filial piety and the archangel who lost the position of servant with a heart of compassion.  
Thus, you must be able to say that you will dedicate your own heart of love and the heart of love that God has not been able to express until now to heaven. If you become those who go this way, you will develop normally in the future. You must clearly understand that you cannot establish the connection between the Father and the son in that position. Do you understand? "Yes."  
<Prayer> Father, the steps I have taken before You until now have been shameful. The sin left by Adam has driven countless people through his descendants to pierce Your heart. We have taken on this historical sin and welcomed the 1970s.  
What path must we take to settle this? Since our human ancestor Adam lost the position of filial piety, we must walk the path of filial piety, and since he lost the position of loyalty, we must walk the path of loyalty. We must first sacrifice for the nation. Until now, we have fought for the nation and the world. Now that we have parents to serve, a path of filial piety has emerged. Father, we must become those who can inherit that path of filial piety and establish the connection of loyalty.  
The path we take for our brothers is not an unhappy path. Even if we find ourselves in a situation like John the Baptist, wearing a garment of camel's hair because we have nothing, we are not pitiful.  
Everything we have can always be dedicated before You, and we can always dedicate our bodies to You.
We are aware that this gathering of ours is a place of joy, and looking back at the past, we realize that we have been so lacking. We sincerely thank you for guiding us without casting aside us, who were so foolish. However, thinking about the many stories that cannot be taught until we pass over the hill of restoration, I truly understand that our Father is a pitiful being.

In this fallen land today, we are in a position where we can at least call you Father and feel your unexpressed emotions, and I cannot express how grateful I am for the grace that allows us to shed tears in this way.

When I think about standing on a foundation built upon countless deaths as offerings and gathering the blood of many grievances, I must feel fear and dread. If we fail, it is not just our own failure, but the failure of our nation and the world. However, we must not forget the bond between the Father and the son. Even if we forget everything else, please let us not forget this. As written in Mark 14, the disciples did not know the inner feelings of Jesus as he prayed. However, today we must realize that we are in a position to speak of such inner feelings of Jesus, and we are in a happier position than the apostles of old.

They went joyfully to the path of the cross, even though they were in a more unfortunate position than we are. Therefore, we, who are in a happy position, must be able to walk the path of being torn and trampled, even if it means walking the path of death, in order to share this blessing. Even if we must die, if we can call out "Abba, Father" like Jesus did, we should not pray to have this cup taken away from us but should strive to walk this path joyfully. I earnestly hope and wish that you will allow us to be your sons who strive to walk this path joyfully.

Father, I hope and wish that every time we come to this place, the hearts of those who seek to find the nation and the world remain unchanged. Whenever I think of them, I hope you will have compassion for them with a heart that sympathizes with the world. You are calling nations through them, seeking the world beyond nations, and seeking to establish your love beyond the world. When I think of you in this way, we must gratefully accept the sacrificial process to prepare that motivation. We must gratefully digest it. I earnestly hope and wish that we can be sons who can do that.

Now, where should these people go? The only paths they can take are the path to the Father and the path to the world of Satan centered around themselves; there are only these two paths. The path for oneself belongs to Satan, and the path of self-denial belongs to heaven.

What a lamentable and miserable fact this is! Since the motivation for the fall was such, please allow us to accept it willingly and move on. Those who seek moments to shed tears of gratitude for heaven by offering themselves and their families as sacrifices are not a holy group? Father, is this not a foundation where you want to pour out all your heart of love? If there are blessed families here, please let them long for such families, love such families, and realize that they were born for such families, living to see the sons and daughters born in those families.

Now, each of us must have an unforgettable moment of connection between the Father and the son that will last for thousands and tens of thousands of years. Was this period such? I earnestly ask and wish that we can return with such a connection.

All remaining lives have already been dedicated before the Father, so let us live without complaints or resentment, quietly walking while being faithful and filial. I earnestly ask that we become your sons and daughters who struggle to sacrifice everything to leave a legacy of the path of love for future generations, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents.
