Planned Operations
Until now, we have not had a foundation to practice on, so we have only been able to carry out innovative activities from time to time. However, this kind of activity system has limitations in moving the whole and connecting each individual to it. Although tens of thousands participated in the recent Asian Victory Conference, when we consider how many members were actually added to our system, it resulted in a very disappointing outcome. While such conferences publicize our church widely, I always feel that they do not significantly contribute to our actual development. The Unification Church has been operating from an intermediate position focused on publicity. In other words, we have been conducting operations to remove the barriers that separate us from society by utilizing public sentiment.

The urgent issues that the Unification Church must solve in the future
However, entering the 1970s, we must surpass that. We must move beyond that era. From this perspective, this year we have raised the banner of "Victorious Unification Front," but we have not yet presented an overall plan or specific content regarding it. While it has been mentioned through some regional leaders, specific content for implementation has not been provided. Even if it were presented, we cannot implement it due to a lack of economic backing.

Considering this issue, while we cannot implement our plans centered around the association, it is a time when you must realize that such times are passing for yourselves. Therefore, as leaders of counties or districts, you are at a point where you must set your own plans to secure a victorious unification front within the scope you currently belong to.

Now, what must we harvest through such operations? It is the numerical increase of Unification Church members. Of course, qualitative growth is also necessary, but how to achieve numerical growth is urgent at this moment. This is because when the nation looks at the Unification Church, it evaluates all our achievements and results based on numerical issues.

However, as a result of years of sacrifice and activity for the nation, we have established an effective foundation that can influence the majority of the citizens. Yet, we are in a position that is too small to actively push forward from that foundation.

Therefore, the biggest issue is how to secure numbers. This is a significant issue that the Unification Church must solve in the future. If we cannot solve this, we will not be able to align with the heavenly fortune that is approaching in the 1970s. You must understand that we are in such an urgent situation.

Next is the issue of economic requirements. Even if many people connect to our system, an organizational structure and planned form must be established to manage them and work together. For this, we need core members and economic backing.

The reasons why the Unification Church has not developed
What is the reason that our Unification Church has not developed until now? The first reason is that the regional headquarters have not been established. This is because regional headquarters may be located in the center of a city or town, but when the contract period ends, they must move. However, considering the economic situation, the value of money decreases year by year. Therefore, what was obtained for 300,000 won may not be obtainable for 500,000 won a year later. With rent increasing every year, the economic burden increases, and as a result, regional headquarters must be moved. It is fortunate if the new location is better, but often it ends up being on the outskirts. When we secure members while in the city, moving to the outskirts results in many members falling away. This is the first reason why the church has not developed.

The second reason is your lack of ability. In other words, as leaders, you have not established a systematic life plan. If there are ten districts in your county, you must have your own plan centered around those ten districts. Also, if there are villages belonging to a district, you must have a plan centered around those villages. Therefore, you must set plans to increase numbers, that is, to evangelize, centered around the villages that can influence the county or the districts that can influence the villages. You must work hard to achieve that plan.

So, what is the method for implementing that plan? The first is principle lectures. We must declare our teachings. We must also conduct victory lectures. However, looking at how you have been lecturing until now, you have been giving partial lectures in various villages, but the range of people you lecture to is limited. In other words, when you lecture on the principles, you are only covering parts of the creation principles and a bit of eschatology and the doctrine of the second coming. This cannot continue. To carry out the operations you have planned, you must prepare a plan for what lectures to give in which places, so that you can lecture on the entirety of the "Principle of Creation." You must plan to implement this. This is something that has not been generally done among you.

In a year, there are twelve months, and in one month, there are 30 days. Within those 30 days, if you have ten places, or even if you have seven, you must go to the places you have planned and give principle lectures. When you lecture, you should change the content each time. This way, you do not have to give the same lecture in one place for a whole year, and you can give different lectures in different places. By alternating your lectures, you can cover the entire "Principle of Creation." You must divide the entire "Principle of Creation" into 12 parts and plan to lecture according to that plan. By doing this, your understanding of the principles will significantly improve.

However, you are lecturing with habitual methods and attitudes. You are only lecturing on areas where you are confident and skilled, and you have not connected those areas with other fields, which is why you have not developed uniformly.

To develop, you must set operational plans.
Now, to fill in these lacking areas, you must plan lectures centered around specific regions or counties. You must also set operational plans for declaring the principles. You must seek a lecture method that can apply the principles to the whole. For this, you must be proficient in both the front and back of the principles. To achieve this, the only way is to give many lectures.

The same goes for victory lectures. You must not always say the same thing. When you lecture, if the audience or the region is different, you should set a title related to that and change the content accordingly. To do this, you must purchase and study all related materials. By planning how to enhance the depth, breadth, and height of your content, you will naturally develop. Because of the inability to lecture in such a planned manner, most people have not developed and remain stagnant. Haven't you spent several years or even over a decade like this?

When you return this time, you must completely renew the methods and perceptions you have been using in the past. Regional leaders must look at the map of their counties and identify how many villages they need to go to. Generally, there may be 200 to 300 villages. Then, you must plan to convey the teachings to each village. In those villages, there are surely prepared individuals who can connect to our purpose, based on the foundation established by the merits of our ancestors. Therefore, you must take on the responsibility to set such people before God, and during your tenure there, you must visit at least three times. You must set such operations and, regardless of the difficulties, take time to conduct circuit lectures.

After conducting the first circuit lecture, the second circuit lecture does not require much more time than the first. The second circuit lecture does not require much more time than the first. From the second lecture onward, specific content is needed. You must organize. If there are people who respond after listening to the lecture, you should return and send them letters. Through letters, you establish a relationship, and you can say that you owe them a favor from your previous visit and ask them to gather the townspeople for your next visit. When you lecture again, you should not repeat the previous content but lecture on something different.

To cultivate skills through the principles
To give such lectures, you must study the principles beforehand. If you are giving a two-hour lecture, you must study for more than two hours. You must pray more than twice as much. Otherwise, you cannot impress the audience.

Here, the purpose of lecturing is not only to convey the message but also to develop yourself. As the number of lectures increases, you must lay a solid foundation for yourself and further solidify the connection of heavenly heart. Based on that foundation, you must be able to influence the whole. You will feel the value of your activities and the source of your motivation increasing. Therefore, the more you continue such activities, the wider the range of your interactions will become, and you will feel your skills improving.

You may sometimes feel emptiness after delivering a message. This means that you have not gained anything through the message. If you simply lecture in the same way as before, what will you feel and what will you gain? However, after delivering the message, you should feel satisfied and realize that you are developing, and that your benefits are increasing. Only then can you continue your activities. Therefore,
In three years, I will reach this level. In five years, I will undoubtedly reach this level. You must gain this confidence. There aren’t many materials needed for your personal development.

So, if you establish relationships and engage with them centered around this environment, it will serve as a foundation for increasing the number of people who follow our intentions, while simultaneously allowing you to develop yourself. When you think about these results, you will never get tired. However, you have been active without this for so long that you become discouraged after just a few years.

Therefore, when you return this time, I hope you will make the most of your time by planning your activities starting from the important places in your village or district. Even if you go to ten districts, do not say the same thing. If you started your principle lecture from the Principle of Creation and the dual characteristics, then next, you should be able to lecture in reverse so that the dual characteristics become the result. You can also focus on the give-and-take action and derive the dual characteristics to lecture. Additionally, you can lecture on the dual characteristics centered around the subject and object based on the three great purposes. You should be able to lecture in various ways like this. Even with just one title of the Principle of Creation, you should be able to utilize the whole content. This kind of training is necessary. By doing so, you can provide something new to those who listen to your lectures, and you will gain the ability to apply the principle lectures in various aspects for yourself.

By doing this, when your relationships in all directions—front and back, left and right, up and down—become higher, deeper, and broader, you will feel satisfaction. The more times you give a principle lecture, once instead of twice, twice instead of ten times, and ten times instead of a hundred times, the more exhilarating you will feel in proportion to the number of lectures given. Also, when you realize that you have the ability to confront anyone with any part of the principle, everyone cannot help but feel joy. It is because you do not feel the joy of your skills improving through the results of such activities that you lose the motivation to want to engage.

Thus, whether in a district or any target area, if you make plans and practice from the perspective of enhancing and cultivating your skills, you will develop infinitely.

However, there will inevitably be issues that arise while giving lectures. If you want to clarify those issues but cannot find them in the principle book, ask the district leader. If the district leader has been active centered on the principle until now, they must have encountered such issues. If they have not encountered them, it means they have failed to fulfill their responsibilities as a district leader. This means they have not fulfilled their responsibilities beyond that of a regional leader.

You are all people who have been in the Unification Church for over ten years, so wherever you are placed, whether you lecture on the entire principle or just the latter part, you should not be blocked. It should itself become a formula. If you become someone who can utilize this as a formula in all phenomena, how vast of a knowledge base will you have? You should find the principle interesting enough to stay up all night reading and bring about development in both intrinsic and practical aspects of your life. However, losing this foundation until now has been a tremendous loss for you. That is how I see it.

So, you should plan your activities centered around the areas or districts you need to engage in. And when giving lectures, do not give the lectures you are good at. Focus on the parts you are not good at, putting in effort and reading something once ten times. Also, try to summarize the key points in various ways. Then, when you lecture, do not start with the best village in the district but rather go to the village with the lowest level and engage with a few people there. Then, you can lecture in the top-tier village. Through doing this once or twice, you can supplement your shortcomings and gain confidence in areas where you previously lacked it. You must have confidence in God's work. You must have confidence. Without confidence, there is no development. From this perspective, you should plan your activities in proclaiming the principle and develop yourselves in relation to the target area.

Planned Guidance Methods for Newly Connected People

Another reason our church has not developed is that we have not maintained interest in the people we have evangelized until the end. We should be increasingly interested in the people we have evangelized as time goes by, but while we are interested when evangelizing, we become indifferent afterward. This is a position that kills the person we have evangelized. It is a killing position. At least for three years, we must maintain interest at all times.

Why? Because that person's spiritual state develops gradually. The position of someone who first heard the principle is different from that of a year later. After a year, they will understand the three-dimensional content of the principle both inside and out. The more they understand, the more they will desire to know about the principle. Therefore, they will want to approach someone who can guide them. If you think of them as family, you must invest more time and create detailed plans to resolve their inner longing. However, if you do not make such efforts and simply say, "Now that you are family, you study," it will not work. You must maintain interest in those who have formed a familial bond for at least three years. 

When a one-year family member and a two-year family member try to walk the principled path, the two-year member will delve into details more than the one-year member. They will want to engage passionately in all areas. You must take care of and nurture such individuals.

The headquarters church has also failed in this regard. Many people have come and gone until now. Initially, they were introduced to the principle to become members, but afterward, they became indifferent. The person who was evangelized liked the principle and, due to the energy of having heard the words, attended the church well for about six months to a year. However, there is no one to guide them, no one responsible. This must be taught by the person giving the principle lecture. After about a year, their understanding of the principle broadens. Their experiential range gradually becomes wider and deeper. Therefore, they want to know more about the principle, but without a subject who can teach them, their curiosity builds up, and they feel the irresponsibility of the members toward themselves. When this accumulates one, two, three times, they begin to self-criticize. As a result, they lose many people.

Doesn't a similar phenomenon occur in the regions? When evangelizing, they work hard, but once they have evangelized and formed a connection with the church, they become indifferent. However, they must be taught and accompanied for at least three years. So, when they face doubts or difficult situations, you must explain it to them in principle, help them understand it in principle, and show them that formal development occurs in this way. Then they will feel that our principle has deep meaning, is great, immense, and wonderful. However, because we do not give them attention, they lose all the environments to have such stimulating experiences. Thus, the initial impression they had when they first heard the principle does not last long. This is like having breakfast but feeling hungry by lunchtime. The impressions they felt do not last long. Therefore, continuous guidance is necessary. If you cannot take responsibility, you must appoint a representative who is connected to the ideal standard of heart you have had while nurturing that person and hand them over.

Responsibilities of Leaders

To give a practical example, this was the report from the ladies who went out to evangelize in the regions. According to one lady's report, about 30 high school graduates from a certain neighborhood came out passionately to follow the principle. These people were fired up and wanted to evangelize, but after 40 days, they returned. If they had continued to send letters and visited them at least once a month after that, they would not have lost a single person. However, after leaving them alone for about ten years, they found that everyone had fallen away. Additionally, there were successors who came and went, but those successors did not inquire about the circumstances of the pioneers or how to guide specific individuals, nor did they ask the pioneer about the emotional stories involved. The regional leader acted arbitrarily, saying, "This is how it is, that is how it is," based on habitual notions. When a sudden outsider comes and tries to take charge, it is different from the person who nurtured them in the past.

The newly appointed leader, having public authority, goes to a place with about 30 members and tries to establish a system based on their own conceptual methods, saying, "Do this, do that." As a result, they lose all the members. They failed to inherit the responsibility from the previous pioneer. This has been the case with regional leaders up to now. From the position of planning and inheriting all emotional and intrinsic matters, they did not place themselves in a position where they could ask for guidance from the members voluntarily, nor did they want to or understand it, yet they said, "Do this, do that." The new leader must be criticized by the members for at least three months. The members are watching them, and they cannot just dictate to the members based on their own convictions. If they do that, there will be side effects within three years. Now, if a new person who has not had any relationship until now is placed in that region and suddenly says, "Do this, do that," problems will arise. At least for three months, they must invest their heart.

Therefore, there have been mistakes in the methods of succession, and the evangelized individuals did not introduce the people they evangelized to the new leader. The leader's actions caused those people to feel disappointed. However, the new leader must support and comfort those who feel disappointed, become a fence for them, allow them to express their difficult stories, and place them in a position where they can move forward with hope for tomorrow. If they do not do this and make them feel disappointed in various ways, they will inevitably fall away. If a member does not attend church three times, problems arise. If they miss one week, two weeks, or three weeks, they become estranged. When they see the leader, they will think, "Ah, I wonder why that leader is not coming to church." If they are asked, they will say they did not come because they felt disappointed, but they will not express their true feelings and will tell a lie instead. If this happens repeatedly, they will gradually drift away from the church and eventually fall away completely.

Thus, while evangelism has been done, many people have been sacrificed due to a lack of follow-up methods. Therefore, it is our responsibility to bear fruit from the people we have connected with rather than just making connections through principle lectures. Thus, what must leaders always think about? The mission of a leader is not to proclaim the words but to reap the harvest. You must understand this. Proclaiming the words is planting, and the mission of a leader is to plant and then reap. For example, you must water the sprouted shoots, do weeding, and ensure that flowers bloom and fruits are borne. Only after a certain period has passed and the harvest is ready can the leader fulfill their mission. However, the new leader should not try to replant what someone else has already planted. They must take good care of it. Even if someone else planted it, if they take good care of it and reap the harvest, it will be stored in heaven's warehouse. However, if they do not have this mindset, do not grasp the character of the previous leader or the overall guidance methods, and instead play around with replanting, they will die. This must not happen.

The Succession Between Predecessors and Successors Must Be Well Established

Because the succession between predecessors and successors has not been well established within our system, many people have been sacrificed. From this perspective, leaders must not only proclaim the words but also become responsible leaders who can reap the harvest. They should not just be planters but must also be harvesters. It takes more than three years to reap. They must not try to harvest immediately. That is why Jesus spent over three years with the twelve disciples. That is the principle. Therefore, you are asked to work hard for three years.

In 1957, the teacher sent out evangelistic teams to 120 locations, saying, "You will serve for three years, and go to the villages to be loyal. What should you teach them? Teach them the way of loyalty. Moreover, show them through practice. Then, even if you do not say anything, they will want to take on what they can." When both you and they come out, you will establish yourselves completely in that village.

However, because they did not fulfill their responsibilities in the regions, it is as if they have built a foundation for a house across the country but have not completed it. Building a house on top of that is more difficult than building a new house. When you go to a place where people have scattered due to previous failures in evangelism and only one person remains, you will have to put in two to three times the effort compared to when you first went out to evangelize. You may have felt this well while pioneering. When we see this, we conclude that we have not fulfilled our responsibilities.

Considering all these issues, we must reassess them. First is the resolution of regional headquarters issues, second is the skill issues in principle lectures, and third is the issue of raising the members we have evangelized. We must not give birth and then abandon them. We must raise them and make them our successors. We have neglected these issues until now. Therefore, as you go to the places you will be responsible for tomorrow, you must plan centered around these issues.

How many people have you evangelized until now? If you have evangelized ten people, you should hold a general meeting with those ten people at least once a year, even if they are scattered in Jeolla-do, Gyeongsang-do, or Gangwon-do. Even if the whole group cannot gather, you should either invite them to meet or create opportunities to visit them at least once a year. You should be able to share your experiences with each other like a parent and child. When a child returns home after being away, they should report on their experiences, and the parents should encourage them, sharing joyful and sorrowful stories based on the emotional bonds of the past. You should have time to connect and share. This can be lengthy.
The longer it is, the more those people will not be able to forget you. However, you have not done such things until now.  
So what have you done until now? When a person who was responsible for the Jeonnam region goes to another place, what they do is send letters to call everyone. This should not be done. You must introduce them to your successor. The introduction must be a personal one. I moved like this, and the person in charge moved like that, so if conflicting phenomena arise, do it this way. If there are still difficulties, then write a letter. This should not be the case. It is not about dragging them to where you are. You must hand them over to the new successor, creating a foundation where they can do even better based on the standards they have been nurtured by you until now. The new person in charge does not know each member of the church well, so that is what I mean. We have not been able to do this until now.  
To have an emotional bond with the members,  
the deep night has a strong sense of mystery. For this reason, even when holding revival meetings, it is more gracious to hold them at night than during the day. This is because during the day, all our emotions are dispersed. In other words, all the senses that we can feel through our five senses are easily dispersed. However, at night, it is not so; rather, it becomes concentrated. Everything surrounds me and highlights me, and because I automatically stand in such a realm, it is easier to experience the work of grace with God at night. God can also work well. Therefore, when you talk to the members in the yard at night, that conversation takes on a sense of mystery. Also, when you talk while taking the members home from visiting the villages, that member will never forget it for a lifetime. The joy of that cannot be described by anything. Those who can live a life where they can feel such value will develop. You should also try to convey the message until you hear the first rooster crow after midnight; how mysterious it is. Try to convey the message while listening to the barking of the neighborhood dogs in the quiet, calm night. It feels like finding a bright sunlight and breaking through a new path in life, like a captain navigating anew by finding the lighthouse light. You will feel a brave, vigorous, and majestic appearance as if you are walking alone in a world filled with mystery. To have this emotional bond, you must guide around the nighttime. Therefore, it is necessary to develop such activities at night or in the early morning.  
However, if the target is married women, problems will inevitably arise. You must make them understand well and respect the nighttime, allowing them to shake off their environment and come out even at night. It is necessary to have this emotional driving force. Thus, you must make those people able to follow your instructions in any environment. This must first be done through the word, then through action, and if it is established emotionally, that person will not fall away. Then, you should try to evangelize. You must raise them to the point where they can evangelize others. If this is done, you will not lose a single person you have evangelized.  
Once you have evangelized someone and they come to church, you should not just leave them alone. When they come to church, give them a topic and have them give a lecture. Let them talk until late at night. This is how you nurture them. By personally evangelizing, they can quickly develop a faith-based character, and they will also feel pleasure. Moreover, by talking to many people, they will gain confidence. Give them more ambitious events or content. If you guide them like this for about three years, they will grow for more than three years. If they jump in directly, they will find their own place.  
Just as parents can truly show filial piety only after having children, by practicing it themselves, they can feel the value of the path we are taking and experience that God is with them. Such people will never fall away. However, we have not been able to create such people until now. This is the reason why the Unification Church has not developed. This is the problem.  
Establish a systematic plan for activities both inside and outside.  
Therefore, to know this content and secure numbers, you must give many lectures. Even when giving lectures, you must do so systematically. You should set a plan to evangelize a certain number of people each month and execute it. Thus, you should aim to evangelize one person per month. This should start from the district leaders and regional leaders. It is possible to do this through lectures. Just going around giving victory lectures is not the responsibility of a leader within our system. After giving a victory lecture, you must give at least two principle lectures. This is a rule.  
However, some people try to give only victory lectures without giving principle lectures. Such people cannot develop normally. Even if they give victory lectures in the future, they will not be able to impress the public and will not be welcomed by the majority. However, if you give principle lectures and base your victory lectures on the emotional content you have experienced in life, you will achieve results. But those who think the opposite will not develop. Their path will inevitably be blocked. Therefore, you must carry out these principles.  
As I have walked through my life until now, when I listen to reports from those who have gone out to evangelize in the regions, it is said that those whom they evangelized with sincerity fall away and must be restored. They mention about ten women who were evangelized by them and worked hard for the purpose but fell away, and when they look at how they got married or settled down, they see that their wives die, commit suicide, their sons die, or they break their legs; it all happens like that. They say they do not know how terrifying it is to see that. It is indeed terrifying.  
So who will take responsibility for that? Those who are in such a position will harbor resentment and hold grudges. Then they will accuse you in the heavenly world. So the problem is serious. It would have been better if they had not been preached to at all. By preaching, it has resulted in them suffering such harm. In other words, if the seeds had not been sown, the core would not have rotted. Such things happen. How terrifying is this?  
Therefore, carelessly preaching the word is also a big problem. If you preach irresponsibly, your own path will be blocked. If a certain number of people suffer such harm, your path will not be easy. You will be bent and broken.  
If the sacrificial offering cannot be a complete sacrifice, what will happen? If the offering makes a mistake, all the people gathered before the altar will also be punished, right? It becomes more sinful than the offering itself. It is like when you come to offer a sacrifice, if the priest makes a mistake in the sacrifice, the attendees bear the sin of the wrongly offered sacrifice.  
Such tremendous things are unfolding before us now. Therefore, you must stand in such a position and be careful with each of your actions and feel a sense of responsibility. You must clearly distinguish between what you should do and what you should not do based on the principles. Therefore, you must establish an official plan centered on the principles and act accordingly. Otherwise, the harm suffered by the other party will come to you indirectly or directly. Then, you will unknowingly lose your strength. Once that happens, no matter how much you try to recover, you will not be able to. Therefore, to supplement what you lack in numbers, you must now establish a systematic plan for activities both inside and outside and strengthen your efforts. You must understand this.  
The next issue is economic. Right now, the most concerning issue for me is how to resolve this economic problem. So you may have received notice that I intend to put the wives of blessed families in each district at the forefront. By collecting the outstanding payments for the air guns assigned to the business departments of each district, we will strengthen the supply by splitting the proceeds with the company.  
What I have planned with this is to supply the material resources we can use for our activities in 1970 through this. Therefore, when you return, you must strengthen the collection activities by putting your wives at the forefront.  
This should not be done blindly. You should set a goal of how much to collect in a month and do it. You should pray and make resolutions together with your wife while guiding them.  
I will evangelize a few people, so you should collect a certain amount. You must plan and work together to secure a new economic foundation. This is also an urgent issue for us now.  
What comes next? The question is how to lay a foundation that can influence the nation based on that foundation. Even if we secure human resources and economic resources, that alone cannot influence the nation.  
So I am thinking about how to influence the nation. Therefore, I am preparing to develop various indirect external activities, including interdenominational activities, to connect this. We must not exceed that standard within three years.  
Thus, you must first establish an operational plan to secure numbers and work hard to lay an economic foundation. In terms of the economic foundation, we must complete the collection of the enormous amount we need to collect this year. I ask you to plan and act on these issues centered around your families. Do you understand? “Yes.”  
If we can proceed like this until the end of 1972, I believe my plans will be realized. By then, we will have considerable human and economic resources before us. If we secure these human and economic foundations, national activities will not be a problem. I am currently planning to bring about such results.  
To supplement the core personnel, I am planning to establish educational institutions. As the first step of this plan, we are holding the first leadership training session this year. This is not only planned for here in Sutak-ri but also for Cheongpyeong. Furthermore, I am not limiting this leadership training to Korea; I plan to train members from Japan, the United States, and Europe together. The training period will be long. I am planning for at least 70 days, more than two months. If they receive training for 70 days, even those who cannot speak English will be able to engage with foreigners in the same living environment, and I believe that those who have graduated from college will be able to converse.  
The question is how to cultivate and deploy global core personnel by creating such training centers. If we can do this well, we will be able to compensate for the mistakes we have made in our activities until now. If we establish such a system and lay an economic foundation, we will be able to move existing churches to some extent. I am currently planning to bring about such global development.  
I ask you to understand this and return to your regions to engage in planned activities. Do you understand? “Yes.” First, we must secure numbers. To do that, we must fulfill our responsibilities as leaders. Next, regarding the economic issue, we must complete the collection of the sales of the guns. I am asking you to do this by putting your wives at the forefront. You should not put church members at the forefront. For four months, put your wives at the forefront. If couples dedicate themselves and put in effort for the purpose, the members who are following will compete to ask to be put forward. Once the collection is completed, even in an environment where no salary is paid, in other words, where there is no economic guarantee, you can have the members do anything. If you do not do this, there will be no way to avoid economic threats in your lives. Therefore, I ask you to set new directions and plans based on these conditions and act accordingly. Do you understand? “Yes.”  
<Prayer> Father, we have learned that the victorious unification front is not made up of just one person. Please allow us to understand that each individual here is a problem.  
First, our bodies and minds must become one. Thus, we must discover the unified self, and based on that self, we must form a unified family with our wives, who are relative beings, and establish a unified form as a couple, centered around our children, so that we can establish a subjective standard that can integrate the families of the satanic world. (The recording was briefly interrupted.)  
As a representative of your character, as a representative of your heart, as a representative of your words, even if the heavens and earth change, we must have a firm and unshakable core authority in this position to influence and digest relative beings, and we earnestly hope and wish that you will help us realize that this is the origin of a new start that can be in harmony with you.  
Father! Now, in the path that the Unification Church is taking, quality is important, but the time has come when quantity is also needed. It is urgent that we have economic support that can use quantity as a fence to expand the organization both inside and outside.  
When we see that there are countless people and material resources in this country, we feel ashamed that we have not fulfilled our responsibilities and have not inherited the authority you have granted us. Therefore, we must seek out those who can connect this. We earnestly hope and wish that you will allow us to become unification warriors who can fulfill the responsibility to establish an economic foundation for these people to live and to set the nation and people in the second liberation realm.  
Father! We thank you for protecting us throughout this Sunday. As we recall all the times we have felt and resolved anew in your connection, please grant infinite mercy and blessings to those who must go to the battlefield tomorrow. While it is important to set our own plans and engage with many people, we must also work harder to nurture our core personnel. By aiming to evangelize one person per month and practicing it, may we feel it as fun and rewarding, and through that stimulation, may we develop and be sons who receive your praise.  
From this moment on, may you personally guard the future path we must take, and may we become workers who plant what we have experienced in the hearts of many people. Not only may we plant, but may we also cultivate and harvest, becoming sons who are loved and praised by you. I ask this in the name of True Parents. Amen.  
Complete restoration.
We must always think that we fallen humans are positioned in between good and evil. Humans cannot cross the boundary without going through this intermediate position. God must work through us, who are in this intermediate position, to cross the boundary, and Satan must also work through us, who are in this intermediate position, to oppose the heavenly side. Furthermore, whether as individuals, families, nations, or the world, we must understand that none can manifest in the providence without taking such an intermediate position.

Fallen humans in the intermediate position of good and evil
When looking at individuals, you have both a mind and a body. If your mind stands in the position of pursuing good, it will touch the boundary on God's side, but if it stands in the opposite position, it will inevitably touch the boundary on Satan's side. Therefore, we must always be aware that we humans are in the intermediate position of good and evil.

This is also true in hierarchical relationships. In considering the relationship between heaven and earth, God must go through humans to occupy this earth. 

February 1970, Tongil Industry Training Center Auditorium.
* This message was given during the first executive training session, but since the exact date is unknown, it is included here. It is also published in <Seonghwa> No. 97 (May 1970).

It is essential that God and humans become one. Additionally, Satan must unite with humans from an earthly perspective to occupy good humans in the heavenly realm. Without this, Satan cannot lead humans in the heavenly realm astray. In this regard, the critical issue is that only in the position where God and we become one can Satan be subdued, while in the position where Satan and humans become one, God must inevitably withdraw.

When examining this in terms of left and right relationships, the relationship of siblings centered on parents is a left-right relationship. Among siblings, a true filial child is one who can treat their siblings while being one with their parents. An unfilial child is one who stands in opposition to their parents and leads the family to ruin. Even when considering the nation, to be a loyal subject, one must unite with the sovereign or ruler and treat the nation accordingly. Conversely, where do treacherous subjects arise? They arise not from uniting with the ruler but from standing in opposition to them, leading to treason.

So how is good and evil determined? Good and evil are determined by whether I lean towards the right or the left; good and evil themselves cannot make us good or evil. It is determined by whether we humans move in the direction of good or evil. Thus, fallen humans are in the intermediate position of good and evil.

Who determines good and evil? It is neither God nor Satan, but rather it is determined by me. Therefore, to return to the side of heaven, I must unite with God. There is no other way. Conversely, if I want to remain in the position of evil, I can only maintain that evil position.

How to escape the fallen realm
So how can I, standing on this fallen foundation today, escape from it? How can I break free? This is the most important issue for fallen humans, who are in the intermediate position and must return to the world of original goodness. The critical question is how I can integrate with goodness.

From the moment I was born with this body until now, I have been accompanied by the evil Satan, and I am in a position where it is easy to continue to be accompanied by it in the future. Everything from one to a hundred is entangled with Satan and evil; it is not in a position to relate to good. We must deny and transcend this evil foundation. To do this, we must pursue a direction or means that can seek good more powerfully than this evil foundation. This is the issue that believers must understand in their lives.

However, if we merely have a vague understanding that God exists and that His will exists, there is no way to resolve this. That is why we emphasize absolute faith. To establish absolute faith, we must go through an absolute process of negation. If I am a citizen of a country, I must be a member of that family, and if I am a man or a woman, I must be a member of a couple, and to advance towards the side of heaven from here, I must proceed centered on absolute faith.

In pursuing absolute faith, even if the nation absolutely opposes it, we must not yield. In the family, no matter how much someone opposes it, we must not be swayed by that opposition with absolute faith. Even in the relationship between husband and wife, we must maintain an attitude of absolute faith even if the other party stands in opposition. The purpose of establishing such an attitude and living a life of faith is to escape the evil environment and return to goodness.

Today, we in the Unification Church know that God exists. This cannot be denied in any way. Through countless testimonies, we cannot deny that God exists. Then, to what extent do I know that God? Is it based on the blind faith that our ancestors believed in? Unless I stand in a position stronger than the blind faith I have pursued, I cannot go beyond the faith of the past. Furthermore, I cannot enter a new world in relation to God, who has been working throughout history.

So what is the problem here? The issue is how to practice as much as we know and how to have a firm conviction to break down all the foundations of evil in reality. We must establish a subjective self that can eliminate the foundations of evil to determine good and evil. It cannot be done solely with God's power.

Evil centered on Satan has an environment that corresponds to 95 percent, while good centered on God has only an environment that corresponds to 5 percent. In other words, God's foundation is less than 5 percent compared to the world of Satan.

In this position, God has been stimulating our conscience and urging the direction of our conscience until now. God has worked historically only when a person decides and when that person can completely become one with God. Even if you pray, you cannot pray from a position of being one with God 24 hours a day, nor can you live a life of faith from that position. Therefore, you must establish a unified trajectory that can connect with the will based on a periodic moment. Only then can you grow and possess autonomy. Until then, you are distanced from God.

You must relate to God and say, "Since God is absolute, I must also be absolute." Since I am in a position to serve God, who has fought for goodness until now, I must stand in a realistic, subjective position and fight centered on the realistic stage.

This belief in fighting must become absolute, looking forward to the time when we can believe in God absolutely and lead our individual selves. When considering whether we stand at such a point, that is the problem. To stand in such a position, we must establish conditions for indemnity. You must understand this.

The teacher who has gone through the process of indemnity
When looking at the teacher himself and reflecting on how his family has lived until now, God is harsh and merciless. At one point, He grants blessings, but… The teacher's family received God's blessing during the time of his great-grandfather. However, during his grandfather's time, they received indemnity. After receiving blessings, they must inevitably receive indemnity. The history of indemnity unfolds after blessings are received. The Israelite people also received blessings and then inevitably faced indemnity. If they received blessings worth ten, they must receive indemnity worth that much. To sustain something and leave behind its seed, they must undergo indemnity. Moreover, to leave a seed for the tribe, not just for the family, Satan pours trials greater than the blessings given to that family. In other words, to give a great blessing, they must also give twenty or even a hundred times the trials. Indemnity must be received.

Thus, until the teacher received God's call, considerable turmoil occurred in his family. Their wealth was squandered, and there were casualties. Furthermore, confusion arose among those on his side. It was said that everything was met with opposition.

When blessings are received, God exposes that family to the world of Satan until they reach a state of despair. Then, they are attacked from the world of Satan. For example, when the teacher sought this will, there were connections of indemnity spanning three generations behind it. Indemnity was received in the grandfather's generation, in the father's generation, and in my generation, including my older brother. Sad events had to occur in the grandfather's generation, and sad events had to happen in the father's generation. Without going through this, indemnity cannot be achieved.

Looking at my grandfather's generation, there were three brothers, and the youngest grandfather was a pastor. He was the overall leader of the March 1st Independence Movement in North Pyongan Province and had been making internal plans with leaders from across the country. He led a mass demonstration with the staff and students of Osan School, church members, and residents of Osan. At that time, he was arrested as a main instigator and spent two years in prison. Even after being released from prison, he could not live comfortably in his hometown and spent his life in exile. Due to persecution from the Japanese, he ended his life in Jeongseon, Gangwon Province. In my father's generation, an uncle also went missing. We do not know where he went. He likely died a tragic death, and we do not know whether there is a grave. Indemnity must go through such a process. In other words, one must go through a life of misfortune. Only after reaching the third generation did the history of normal struggle finally begin. In other words, the foundation for restoration was established.

My older brother was absolute towards me, the younger brother. An expectation was naturally formed that he could completely indemnify from Cain's position. My brother's faith was thorough. He foresaw the outbreak of the Korean War and also anticipated our nation's liberation. He had an attitude of faith that resolved all difficult problems through spiritual guidance. My brother had a spiritual illness, which was unavoidable. However, he never thought about using medicine to cure it. He overcame the illness solely through prayer and faith. It was from that standard of faith that he healed that illness.

My brother knew that, regardless of anything else, I was a historical younger brother among the many older brothers and younger brothers throughout history. Therefore, he absolutely obeyed me. When I was in Pyongyang, it was a time when a significant history was unfolding in the providence of restoration, and what I asked for was something that could not be believed in ordinary thinking, but my brother helped me for my sake, equipped with various details. No matter how difficult the request was, he did not hesitate to carry it out.

Thus, we became separated. The North and South were divided. The circumstances of our family expanded into the circumstances of the nation. Just as the older brother and younger brother could not gather to serve their parents, the current situation of North and South Korea is the same. Without a doubt, my brother was likely killed by the North Korean regime. Moreover, because I am out in South Korea doing this work, our relatives remaining in North Korea must be living in unspeakable suffering and adversity, having either died or still living that way. When viewed in light of historical processes, it is inevitable that such a process must be gone through.

Even in the teacher's case, all the closest friends who could bless him from heaven were taken away. Everything that could be relied upon in the world was cut off. Among them were people from North Pyongan Province and Hwanghae Province. All the closest friends were taken away.

Furthermore, looking at siblings, my most beloved younger sister was taken away. While I was in prison, for reasons unknown, she was taken away. She is my younger sister, just below me. Our family had many daughters, but my aunt had no daughters, so at my aunt's request, that sister went to live with her. Therefore, the teacher always prayed a lot for that sister. That sister was absolute towards her older brother. So, I thought I should do anything that would be good for her as an older brother, but even that expectation was cut off. Not only my younger sister but also my beloved younger brother was taken away. Additionally, among the teacher's children, Heejin, who is the younger sister of Seongjin, was also taken away. In terms of sons, it was like the second son was taken away. The second daughter was also taken away. When looking at this, indemnity is unforgiving. The teacher is not an exception.

The position of indemnity
When did I suffer the most on this path of will? It was during the second path. Of course, the first path was the same, but the second path was even more so. Such a process was unavoidable.

Heaven and Reality
<Prayer> Father, we must surely understand that we must conclude what Jesus had to establish 2,000 years ago in connection with the Jewish people today.

Father, today is the second Sabbath in March, so please bless this day. This morning, may you be with us in your heart of love, and allow us to understand that you are personally watching over our life journey, and that we must also become necessary beings in the world you desire.

We must understand what you are seeking in ourselves, our families, our nation, our world, and the universe. However, we have come to realize that it is difficult to establish a relationship with you if we only understand it conceptually. Today, we must consider how we live centered on our families, nations, and the world, and whether we are the ones who motivate ourselves or whether you are the one who motivates us; we must establish one of these relationships. Without this, we must surely understand that we cannot reach the world of good results that you desire.

Father, when we think about ourselves once again, even if we are called to stand before your will, we must become those who can receive your love, align with your heart, and eternally accompany your heart.

We must pursue the way to become gods. When we pursue such a figure, we will discover that we started from evil. Please remove such traces and allow us to discover the contents that can align with your heart, your body, your life, and your ideals during this time.

May our worldly hearts transform so that they can align with such contents. Thus, we earnestly hope and desire that we may become entities that can bring forth the results of goodness that you need.

As we enter the 1970s, we are each walking with the banner of a victorious unification front. Now, after nearly 70 days, let us reflect once again on where we have set out and what steps we have taken. May we question ourselves whether our steps and our actions are in line with the direction and standard that you have set as your goal, and when we find ourselves in a position that does not align, may you push us to ensure that we can align and proceed in the direction and standard that you desire, Father, we earnestly hope and desire.

As we reflect on the past 360 days, we must have a heart of gratitude to you rather than a heart of despair regarding the results we have encountered. Thus, when we can stand in a position to say, "We have established the standard you desired for all the world, so please accept us," we must know that this position is not a position of hardship but a position of joy and glory. We must understand that such a position is not created by chance without our own thoughts.

**Our Mission**

We know that the world in which humans live is not a world that can be controlled by human hearts. In the case of the Republic of Korea, it cannot control Asia at will, and Asia cannot control the world at will either. From this perspective, we realize that this world, too, is in a position where it cannot control heaven and earth.

**Starting Point of Restoration History**

When looking at individuals, when a family is placed before an individual, and a tribe before a family, and a nation before a tribe, in order to control the larger entities, a foundation of victory must be established. Without that, one cannot exercise dominion. Furthermore, to unify these, it is clear that one must pay a greater price than what is presented.

In daily life, when you plan a task in the morning, to accomplish that task, you must have a greater internal resolution than the task itself. However, no matter how resolved you are internally, if you do not solve the relative problems that must be addressed in the environment, you cannot say that you have successfully completed your day's work. You cannot enjoy the glory of being a victor.

Just as it is with individuals, the same process applies to nations and the world; to have the authority to exercise dominion, one must pay a greater price.

Moreover, the restoration providence does not originally start from the nation. It does not begin from the nation to the world. It starts from the individual, then to the family, from the family to the tribe, from the tribe to the nation. We must think that we need to develop this to the world or to heaven.

God, who is carrying out the restoration providence, is also in a position where He cannot freely exercise dominion over individuals. Because there are greater tribes before individuals, a greater sacrifice must be paid to restore individuals. Without that, individuals cannot be restored. This is an undeniable fact when viewed through the historical process. We are well aware that the restoration historical process has been like this.

**Standard of Completion of Restoration Providence**

Why is this so? It is because the forces of Satan, which have a greater foundation than individuals, are connected to individuals. Therefore, to restore individuals, one must pay a greater price than the individual. To find Abel, one had to pay a price of more than double, and to establish Noah, one had to lay a foundation of absolute authority to overcome all environments before the national authority. It took a period of 120 years to establish that foundation. The same goes for Abraham.

To save individuals, the issue is not the individuals themselves but how to overcome the environment connected to those individuals. This is true for Jacob, Moses, and Jesus. When it comes to saving individuals, one must overcome the realm of Satan and subdue Satan. To overcome that environment, one must pay a greater price of trials, indemnity, and sacrifice than that environment itself.

From this perspective, where is the standard of the Unification Church's mission? When centered on the issue of individual restoration, there is a mission to pay a price of indemnity greater than the individual, and this is also true when centered on the family. Furthermore, the restoration of heaven requires the ability to actively restore based on a standard greater than that title. Without that, it is impossible.

For example, to cut something with a sword, the sword must be stronger than the object. Otherwise, it cannot cut the object. Similarly, to fulfill the restoration providence, one must have the proactive ability to overcome all relative conditions that arise. In other words, one must become strong. Thus, when the self is struck by the other, it must be in a position to break the relative existence without being broken itself. Otherwise, there will be no completion of the restoration providence.

In this regard, the struggle to overcome individual issues today is also a battle, and the same goes for families, tribes, and nations. We must also recognize that there are environments of struggle waiting for us centered on nations and the world. Therefore, the struggle we engage in is different from the struggles of today's human world. First, we must overcome and win against the invisible world of Satan. Only then can we win against the tangible world of Satan. We must subdue the spiritual Satan before we can subdue the substantial Satan.

The position we bear, which carries the mission of fighting on the front lines we are facing today, is not a one-sided position. We possess a dimensional position that ranges from a flat position to a three-dimensional one. The path we must take is one that must first overcome the dual world centered on the spiritual and physical realms and advance straight toward that purpose. We must understand this fact.

God has been fighting to overcome various problems on this earth from a proactive position in the spiritual world. However, even if God stands as a victorious standard in the spiritual world, if He does not engage in the path to overcome the problems of the physical world centered on human beings, He cannot have the authority of victory on earth. This is a fact we have learned well through the process of the restoration providence.

So how do we, as fallen humans, overcome this dual world? God has gone through 6,000 years of history to overcome the issues of the substantial physical world. When we think about this, we realize that we are not standing in a proactive position like God, but rather we are surrounded by the realm of the fall, and how we complete this dual struggle is an incredibly serious issue.

**We Must Establish a Standard of Victory**

Therefore, we first need a standard of victory. We need a starting point from which we can carry out our mission. What does this mean? It means that in establishing a standard of victory, one must not belong to any relative existence but must establish that standard from a proactive position. Otherwise, it is natural logic that one cannot realize the intended purpose. So where do we establish this standard of victory? It must be established within ourselves. This is the issue.

When Jesus came to this earth and stood as the responsible person to carry the entire mission of God and complete the battle that unfolded in heaven, what was always at the center of the issue? It was God and Jesus Himself. God had to be the center of the universe, and Jesus had to be the center of reality. He always kept this in mind. If a gap opens here, and conflicts arise centered on a single purpose, one cannot advance in the direction of victory. This is a defined principle.

That is why what Jesus always deeply pondered in his heart was that the Father and the Son must always be one.
It was recognized that in order to establish a victorious foundation centered on God, who is the victorious subject, I must first hold God in my heart from a subjective position while on earth. From this perspective, we can understand that Jesus’ statement of being the temple of God is valid. Ultimately, the standard of victory is a foundation that becomes one with the temple, centered on Jesus, who embodies God on earth. We must understand that without establishing a standard of victory, there is no way to conclude the restoration or to fulfill Jesus’ mission at that time.

Therefore, Jesus did not say that the kingdom of heaven is in the spiritual world. He said it is in your heart. Thus, He emphasized that you must first hold the source that can be the motivation for victory in your heart. In that kingdom, there will be God, God’s family, God’s lineage, God’s nation, and God’s world; the kingdom of heaven is not elsewhere but in your heart. He spoke this way because He understood better than anyone that humans must determine the standard of victory within themselves.

“Repent! The kingdom of heaven is near.” But where is the kingdom of heaven near? It is not near the earth, but near your heart. Therefore, unless you first establish that standard in your heart, the kingdom of heaven, no matter how close it is to the earth, cannot relate to you, nor can it relate to your parents, nor to your sons and daughters. The standard must first be established in your heart.

From this perspective, without establishing a standard of faith and starting from there, no matter how long one has practiced their faith or how difficult their path has been, they cannot be said to have reached a position equipped with the standard of victory. Thus, the biggest issue is that one must have a moment to first determine the standard of victory within themselves.

How should we establish a standard of victory? Today, we who stand on the path of restoration must reflect once more on the countless ancestors who fought for restoration in the past but failed, flowing into emptiness along with history. However, the hopeful standard we should look at from the perspective of following the path they took is not the national or ethnic standards they looked toward. We stand before a global standard that can surpass such criteria. When we think centered on this self, the question arises: How shall I go?

In the past, our ancestors did not achieve primary victory before their purpose and left behind a history of sorrow as losers. Thus, they are not objects of admiration today but are in a position to be criticized. Where does this cause lie? It lies in their failure to establish a standard of victory that can always align with God.

Therefore, we must understand how to establish such a standard of victory. And in practicing that understanding, one must be courageous and have self-confidence. Furthermore, if there are those who oppose that self, one must become a courageous person who can attack and overcome them. Otherwise, all the standards one has struggled to gain knowledge or practice until now will become relatively misaligned. Thus, when there is something that hinders the direction one is heading, one must decide how to establish and practice a solution that can overcome it all at once with the skills and achievements one has built up. Only then can our mission and responsibilities be fulfilled.

So why did our ancestors fail in the past? They lacked a knowledge base regarding the standard that could fulfill God’s desired purpose in the process of restoration. They did not know. Moreover, even what they knew, they could not practice.

One must not only practice and bear fruit but must bear fruit simultaneously with practice. Therefore, practice requires training and preparation. No matter how much one knows, without practice, that knowledge will not benefit them. For this reason, knowing and practicing must become one. Only then can relationships be established. Relationships are formed through the conditions of the other party, so in an independent position, terms like relationship or connection cannot be established.

Thus, knowing alone does not resolve everything. After knowing, one must practice. To succeed, one cannot just practice once. Doing so makes failure easy. Hence, training is necessary here.

If someone participates in a marathon, they know how the course is laid out, how long it will take, how far it is, and from where to start and in which direction to run. When the race starts, all the athletes will be at the starting line, and sometimes a person named A will run ahead, and sometimes a person named B will lead. They also know where the turning points are and where the finish line is.

Everyone knows this. However, to actually win, what must one do? One must train to run faster than anyone else to reach the destination. Without becoming such a person, one cannot win. The same applies to the providence of restoration. It is not enough to just know; one must practice.

Therefore, when we look at the Unification Church today, the concern is not that we do not know the principle itself, but rather what and how we will practice after knowing it.

When comparing knowing and practicing, which is more difficult? Knowing is easy. A smart person can memorize an entire book of principles with little effort. However, practicing is difficult. Practice must be done with one’s life on the line. Knowing can be prepared over a period of time, but practicing requires one to invest their life. It is not enough to just move one’s hands or feet a couple of times or to just go back and forth. That will not bring about the providence of restoration.

Why? Because the connection of the providence of restoration is not completed by moving any part of oneself. It starts from the foundation of individual victory. It begins from the individual who has won and fulfilled their mission; one cannot start from below that level. Therefore, one must go to the position where they can win as an individual, even if it means sacrificing their life. It will not suffice to think that one can just do it adequately over a few days or years. One must fulfill individual restoration. There is a limit to this. This cannot be avoided.

Then, when crossing this limit, does one do it alone? As mentioned earlier, even if restoring a nation, it cannot be done solely by that nation; it must be done through the world. Thus, we must go from the individual to the world.

In this perspective, an individual connected to the providence of restoration does not end at the individual level. There must be a family involved. Why? Because the fall is connected to the family. The motive for the fall was the individual Adam and Eve, but because they brought it into the family, it resulted in dragging the lineage into it, the nation, and the world.

Therefore, the problem here is the limit centered on the individual. A limit centered on oneself is not acceptable. It must be a limit that stands in a position transcending the world. This is because the connection is linked to the world.

The American people and the Korean people are the same. When looking at developed and developing countries, one can find many superior individuals in developing countries compared to developed countries. There are illiterates and beggars in America, just as there are professors and beggars in Korea. A professor in Korea is better than a beggar in America. However, when looking at the entire population, Korea cannot shake off the label of being a developing nation. Yet, a beggar in America is labeled as a citizen of a developed country. Why? Because the difference in the range of what is established influences the character of individuals.

What determines the standard of character that can appear in the history of the providence of restoration today? It is not determined by you but by the established victorious standards of the providence of restoration. The victorious standard stands in a position that can naturally subdue the world. When such a victorious standard of Adam and Eve emerges, from that Adam and Eve, families, lineages, nations, and the world begin to form. Thus, from this perspective, when you work, the ideology of unification is necessary. The ideology of unification is centered on the concept of Godism. Godism is a thought centered on a transcendent worldview that we can personally possess. So, when we stand in such a position, what happens? It is a position based on the original human before the fall, not within the realm of the fallen. And when God recognizes that, there will be content and motivation to resolve all matters.

However, while there is content and motivation, the question remains as to how to bring about results. Therefore, one must not just move adequately with their thoughts elsewhere. One must make a decision, a resolution.

Those who have come and gone on the path of restoration should not think they can just follow along casually. They must be resolute in their connection to the purpose. Everyone must understand that they must practice resolutely. Thus, to transcend one’s personal limits, you must think about how to do so.

The 6,000 years of history thus far is a history of finding one Adam. It is a history of recreating one Adam. Therefore, you must follow me. Eve cannot be created without Adam. To find that one, to create it, the blood and flesh of countless people who have come and gone on the path of restoration must serve as the material. Even though they are in the spiritual world, by establishing a relationship with the reality on earth, they too will experience liberation. This must not be vague or abstract. The issue is how to achieve this awareness.

When Jesus fasted for 40 days, Satan said, “If you are hungry, turn these stones into bread.” At that time, Jesus replied that man does not live by bread alone but by the word of God, centering on God. Then Satan tested Jesus again. He placed Jesus at the top of the temple and said, “If you are the Son of God, throw yourself down.” At that time, Jesus said, “Do not put the Lord your God to the test.” To test Jesus regarding the world, Satan took Him to a high mountain and said, “If you bow down and worship me, I will give you all the kingdoms of the world.” To this, Jesus replied, “Get behind me, Satan! Worship the Lord your God and serve Him only.”

In this way, Jesus was tested by Satan regarding the word, the reality, and the world. This was a test that Satan posed to Jesus, who was in the principle, but the content is a test regarding the word, the reality, and the world that we must also undergo.

So where lies the problem? When Satan told Jesus, “If you are the Son of God, jump down,” it was as if he was saying, “If you are the Son of God, shouldn’t you overcome the realm of the fall? If you are the Son of God, shouldn’t you win in my test?” This implies that if Jesus came to this earth as the Son of God, then none of the conditions of suffering that God faced in the process of restoration should exist within Jesus.

From this perspective, the 6,000 years of history has been a training to restore Adam. So what happens after restoring Adam? It is to create Eve. But one must not leave them like the Adam and Eve of the Garden of Eden. They must be managed well and guided properly. If they go east, they must go east; if they go west, they must go west, and they must always be well-managed nearby. You are currently in such a position. The blessed families today are like Adam and Eve.

All humans in the world of Satan are like archangels. They are like fallen archangels. Thus, when standing in the position of fallen Eve and fallen archangel, they must manage how to do so well when they are in the position of Adam and Eve before the fall.

You too are in such a position. Do not think that there are many people in the vast universe. There are 3 billion people in the world, but they are all our enemies. How can parents traditionally instill their thoughts into their growing children?
