You must bear this double cross.

The method to restore Cain.
You should not be ambivalent or indecisive right now. You must unite internally and step forward to save families and nations from the world of Satan. When you take initiative, your family becomes like the temple of God. In other words, it is like an altar. Therefore, when you pray, you should say, "Father, please love my family and my nation even more than you love me." You should not just say, "Father, help me." A clever person prays for those who are close to God. They are the ones you should rely on. Even if someone is very close to God, they will be caught up in that connection, and just being with them will bring blessings.

That's how religion works. When we believe in Jesus and pray before God, we do so in the name of Jesus because He is closer to God than anyone else. You should say, "Please do this for Jesus because He must have wanted it. Why wouldn't you do it?" This is the kind of prayer you should be making. Asking for blessings while following Jesus is like selling Him out, but that is how it happens.

Therefore, when you pray, you must always invoke those whom God loves. Isn't that the method to restore Cain, who stands in the position of the fallen archangel? That's right. God will welcome that. If you reject this, then the history of restoration must fail. This principle requires that you must sell out Jesus.

"God, doesn't your son want this? Doesn't your son want this nation and this world? Isn't this the wish of your sons and daughters, and your wish as well? If it is necessary for the nation and the world, please allow me to die." For the sake of this world, for the will of your son, I must go. This is how it must be done.

What makes Christianity different from other religions is that the Father, Son, and Holy Spirit are one. This is wonderful. If you are chased away by the Father, there is the Mother, and if you are chased away by the Mother, there is the beloved son. How wonderful is that? Therefore, we who stand on the path of restoration today must lay down our own bridges to reach there.

So how do we find a victorious standard for ourselves today, and how do we cross the boundary? We must always invite God. In other words, we must welcome God, who is the center of spiritual victory. Then, God and I become one. However, I am too far from being one with God. God is at a holy standard, but I am as far from that standard as I am fallen. There is a distance. That is why I am distant from God.

So how do we bridge this distance? What is needed here are the prophets who have come and gone on the path of restoration. Why? Because if it is Abel, we must lay down Abel as a bridge; if it is Noah, we must lay down Noah; if it is Abraham, we must lay down Abraham; if it is Moses, we must lay down Moses; if it is John the Baptist, we must lay down John the Baptist; if it is Jesus, we must lay down Jesus as a bridge. To lay down these bridges, we must walk the path of becoming one with them. To walk that path, we must dedicate our lives.

Some people say they will fight for their nation, while others say they will fight for the world and the universe with love and dedicate their lives. Who will inherit God's great work? The one who says they will dedicate their life for the world and the universe will inherit it. Do you understand what I mean? That is how it will be.

When we look at Jesus, who fought on the cross, His death was for the sake of finding the nation. Therefore, you must go out to find the world for Him. Because you live for Him, you can connect with Him. However, if you die while living for yourself, you become a traitor.

Look to the world and go out. You must find the nation He is looking for and the world. It is natural to find the nation along with Him, and if you do so, that nation will be saved. Then, you must inevitably follow those who have dedicated themselves to finding that nation and the world. That is how it is.

Why must it be so? If it doesn't happen in one generation, it must be restored in the second generation. Who can restore Adam? It is Adam's son. Who can resolve God's resentment? It is God's son. Then, who can stand one step ahead? It is not the subject but the object. The object can stand one step ahead. When a person is beaten, it is the flesh that gets hit first, not the bones.

Therefore, you must go out to find the nation and the world for Jesus. Then, many people will seek the way to find that world. So, why is the world in its current state? Because there is a problem with the leaders who can guide the world.

A person who can guide the world must establish a victorious standard and stand in a position centered on heaven and earth. However, even if such a person emerges, that one person alone cannot fulfill the will. If that person is the only one, they will have to fight against the world of Satan centered on that person. They must fight with the conviction that the world will follow within one century. If the world is not restored in one century, then it must be done in the second century, and if not in the second century, then it must be done in the third century. That is how it must be done.

Therefore, even if a religious leader or a national leader who had such aspirations dies in this first century, everything will not end with their death; even after their death, they can still subdue the world of Cain. 

They fought for the nation, but what I want to find is the country and the world. As long as there is someone who steps forward with that mindset, it is fine. The former is the appearance of a son, but the latter is the one who fights for this world and for heaven and earth, standing in a representative position on this earth as a global figure, fulfilling their responsibilities as a center in the spirit world. If they do so, any religious leader who has come to this earth and gone to the spirit world must follow that person and promote the restoration movement.

So, who does God raise up? He raises up those who struggle to fulfill their mission of individual restoration, rather than those who merely struggle for personal restoration. God needs such people.

From this perspective, individual victory is an unending victory. For an individual to rest, there must be the fence of a family. An individual within a family can rest, but an individual without a family cannot rest. Furthermore, for a family to rest, it must establish the standard of a tribe and have the protective rights of that tribe. Without that, it cannot rest.

You have heard these words until now, but you cannot develop without practice. However, do not think that what you will do in the future is impossible due to your abilities, and do not worry.

Let’s say the nation is in a state of emergency, and the fate of the country is at stake. If there is a death-row inmate who has violated the national law, and that inmate goes into enemy territory and beheads the enemy leader, then there arises a motive for the enemy nation to fall. In that case, the death-row inmate has made a greater contribution to the nation than the crimes they have committed, so all their sins will be erased, and they will be honored. Isn't that right?

What this means is that you must seek where your path lies in your current work. You should not have the mindset that you are only fighting to save this nation in the providence of national restoration. The end of your gaze should be the world, and you must have the thorough mindset that you are fighting for that world. In other words, if you have the attitude to face difficult realities centered on an overwhelming purpose, you will not fail. And if the nation falls, you must advance with the thought that there is another stage for the fight for the world.

In this light, do not speak trivial words about believing or not believing in God's providence centered on a greater purpose. Saying you cannot do it is trivial.

Here lies the foundation that can build the world, that is, the key to conquering the world is right where you live. If there are people who are weary or complaining about the process of restoration, they will not remain for tomorrow. Even if they do remain, they will not be of help to the world of tomorrow.

The standard for fulfilling our mission
The teacher has said that he is one era ahead of you. Likewise, a wise person will think about what the purpose of God's providence for restoration is. They will also worry about what kind of world God desires at the end of the world, and what God will require of us when that time comes. For such a person, even if the world flows away and perishes, a time will come when they can be resurrected.

Jesus, being such a person, died centered on that world, the world after the end times, and therefore the world of the end times could not dominate Him. That is why He became the new protagonist of history. He is not the protagonist of the history that has passed but the protagonist of a new historical era.

His thought is not the thought of the historical era up to that point, but a thought that transcends historical eras, so the era that Jesus desires will surely come. It is a thought that is for the individual, for the family, for the tribe, for the nation, for the world, and for something greater. Today's humanity cannot go without severing that historical connection. That is why we must inevitably submit before such a central thought. You must understand this.

Now, when we look at the Unification Church, the teacher says, "Let’s do this," and you respond, "Yes." But how should you do that well? If you are responsible for a region, you must be loyal to that region. But does that mean you should only do well in your assigned region and not be loyal to the nation? No. Doing well in your region is a process of doing well for the Republic of Korea, and being loyal to that region is a process of being loyal to the Republic of Korea. It is not only for the Republic of Korea but also for the world and for God. This is layered in multiple ways.

That is why, even if the work you do in a small region is small, it is training. Training is for practical application. You are currently being trained. What is that training for? It is for being loyal to the Republic of Korea. However, the standard for fulfilling our mission in the fight we are engaged in is for the world. Therefore, training is essential. You must clearly understand this. It is still a time for such training. Yet, do you still think you cannot do it?

Some of you may think that if you did not know the principle, you would have already run away, but since you know the principle, you cannot do it. Such people also call upon the Father in prayer. However, that Father is not just the Father who deals with you one-on-one; He is the Father who encompasses the world.

You are not just the sons of that Father. To become the sons of that Father, you must be able to enter into the world that He encompasses. Is that place where all 3 billion people of the world can enter? No. It is a place where only one person can enter. That is why the place of work is one, and the territory of work within a day is also limited. Then how do you connect that limitation with the world?

The Final Time and I
When we reflect on the providence of restoration, we come to understand that the term restoration is not originally a noun that humans desired in their original creation, but rather a noun that became necessary as a result of human fall. We must understand that this has caused not only humans but also heaven and earth to be in sorrow.
If there was a world of original creation where restoration was not needed, we can imagine that there would come a time when the fallen world would need to be restored. In this light, it is needless to say that there must be a time when the providence of restoration can be completed.
A Time of Hope and a Time of Misfortune
When God created heaven and earth, there was no need for restoration. The hope that God had centered on Adam in the world of original creation is fundamentally different from the hope that is longed for in the world that must be restored today. The ultimate hope in creating Adam and Eve was to manifest God Himself. In other words, through Adam and Eve, God wished to unfold His internal elements as an external reality, hoping to reach a time when His grand hope and humanity's hope would align.
March 12, 1970 (Thursday), Unification Industry Dormitory Auditorium.
* This message was given at the 2nd Association Executive Training Session.
289 
In this light, it is needless to say that Adam and Eve were created to connect themselves to God's hope. Until the moment before their fall, Adam was in a position where he could be in harmony with God and also in harmony with God's hope, but from the day of the fall, he lost the position to be in harmony with God and the position to be in harmony with God's hope. This is the fallen position.
Because humanity is in such a position, it is an unbearable fact in the history of heaven and earth that God must look upon fallen humanity. No matter how conceptually sorrowful or unjust it may seem, when we consider what content causes such unbearable sorrow, we find that there is content beyond our imagination.
When God sent His beloved only son into unfortunate circumstances to find His original position, and then found Himself in the position of having lost that child, the pain that God experiences is beyond words. Until one experiences such a situation, it cannot be understood through explanation. However, while such experiences should not happen to you, is it not necessary to seek a level of experience that can understand the sorrow God felt due to humanity's fall?
Children do not know how much their parents love them. The dimension of a child who thinks that their parents love them based on their own following and liking is different from the dimension of a parent loving their child. Because God established an absolute standard that He could never create again, Adam and Eve were created, and from the moment they fell, humanity has been unable to start on its own, which is an absolute principle.
God hoped for a time of fulfillment, but due to the fall of Adam and Eve, He encountered a time of misfortune. This is the reason why the history of misfortune has unfolded until now.
290   The Final Time and I
The question is how God can remove the painful heart caused by this fall, and how humanity can resolve this miserable fate and return to its original position. In other words, the problem is how we can liberate ourselves who are bound by eternal chains, and how God can remove the pain in His heart.
When will there be a time to comfort the sorrowful God?
Then who can solve this problem? Humans have spouses, children, and relatives, so when they encounter sorrowful circumstances, they can receive comfort and overcome those circumstances. However, there is no such environment or anyone for God.
You can receive comfort when someone in a more painful position than you comforts you. However, because God is experiencing more sorrow than anyone else, there is no one who can comfort God. Since God is both the beginning and the end, the question is how to resolve the resentment that is bound in His heart; this has been God's internal situation until now. God has carried out the providence of restoration with this situation in mind.
The spirit world transcends time and space, so the sorrow from 6,000 years ago remains forever within the historical realm. If one has felt joy through the experience of offering oneself as a sacrifice, it will not be forgotten in their lifetime, whether it is a matter of time or living conditions. As time goes on, the breadth and depth of that experience grow, becoming an object of reverence, and it connects to an infinite source. In the future, when you have such spiritual experiences and carry out such content, you will understand that the sorrow God has endured until now is not temporary but has been continuously connected. This is an undeniable fact.
God has not found a way to relieve the sorrowful heart until now and remains with that heart. Yet, even while wandering in the fallen environment today and being in miserable circumstances, God forgets Himself to liberate humanity and works from the position of a parent. You must understand how miserable God is in such a position.

The Providence of Restoration Centered on the Families of Adam and Noah
We know that history has flowed for 6,000 years until now. We also know that there have been numerous twists and turns in this process of restoration history. God earnestly wished to restore what Adam had failed through Abel, but what was God's heart at the moment Cain killed Abel? It was despair.
It is already sorrowful that Adam fell, but when Cain killed Abel, who was the hope of restoring the lost children, God had to face the failure of the second hope of restoration and left deeper wounds in His heart. We must understand that humanity's ancestors are the origin of sorrow before God, and Abel's brutal murder inflicted further wounds on God. God has come forth with this accumulated resentment.
The same was true for Noah. He walked a path of suffering for 120 years. He was pushed into a lonely position where no one could follow him. Whether ordinary or specific, any fallen human could not reach the level Noah was driven to.
Noah had to be driven to that point. Why? Because he could not go to a place where there were two. He had to go to a place of solitude. Without entering such a place, restoration cannot be achieved.
In this way, Abel also faced God alone in his own place, and Noah also faced God alone in his own place. Although Adam and Eve were created as two individuals, providence is centered around the man. 

When we look at the history of restoration, it is a principle that the man must find this. Therefore, in the process of restoration, the place Noah goes to must also be a place where only God and Noah himself can meet. The question is how to carry out such a realm. 

In this regard, Noah must establish a relationship that can become one with the goal planned and directed by God, creating an absolute relationship. Noah had to establish a condition of indemnity that could align with God, the subject, from a position similar to that of the manifested reality of God. For this reason, we must understand that God wanted Noah to establish an absolute standard of faith for 120 years and pushed him forward. It was not just one day or ten years, but a period of 120 years. However, during that time, God did not always come to Noah to tell him to endure and overcome. Once he believed, he should have been able to keep that determination forever, and once he believed, he should have become someone who could transcend any shaking of the environment. 

From that standpoint, Noah faced the judgment of the flood after the 120 years. Noah believed that from here, there would be a new fulfillment of God's wishes. However, when viewed from the perspective of Noah, it could not be restored through Noah alone. Just as Adam needed his son Abel to be restored, Noah’s son must establish a standard that can align with his father to restore the fallen relationship of the father and son, and without that, he cannot prepare the attitude to enter the original world. The child is the one who initiates the providence of salvation. Originally, it was supposed to be the father, but because of the fall, it became the responsibility of the child. 

For this reason, in the providence centered on Noah, he had to go through all the trials and adversities to establish a standard where the father and son could be united, which is why the flood judgment lasted for 40 days. After the judgment, on this earth, there were only the father and his family, and there was no one who opposed them. God's providence centered around Abraham, Moses, and Jesus
This was also the case centered on Abraham. It was not easy until God commanded him to leave Ur of the Chaldeans, raising the son of Terah. Choosing Abraham, who grew up in a habitual living environment and had many experiences, was not an easy task. God came with all the internal sorrows that had been present in the historical process up to that point and raised Abraham to resolve that sorrow. 

For this reason, He commanded him to take his beloved son, who was in the hands of the enemy, to leave his homeland and walk the path to Egypt. The moment Abraham offered the sacrifice was a moment of hope for God, who had gone through 2,000 years of suffering after Adam's fall. However, due to Abraham's mistake in offering the sacrifice, he left behind a grudge that required a third restoration. 

Moses was able to resolve this as he led the people out. God raised Moses to guide the nation, but Moses failed by striking the rock twice while leading the Israelites out. Thus, God sent John the Baptist ahead of Jesus to prepare the way, and when Jesus came, He sent the Magi from the East centered around Joseph's family. The purpose of sending the Magi was not to testify about Jesus. It was to have them bow before the Messiah, who was coming as a representative of a nation, and the gifts presented by the three Magi were to restore what the three archangels could not submit to God and Adam. Although the Magi brought gifts to Jesus, what Jesus needed was not the gifts. It was not the gifts as conditions, but the reality of the Magi that was needed. The Magi, who were specially chosen by God to cross borders, should have informed the Israelite nation of the birth of the righteous one and guided them.

In other words, there was an initial conceptual stage. He must have envisioned the entire universe He wanted to create in His heart and thought about creating the world of the object to be manifested, that is, the world of reality, step by step.

The Bible says that God created the created beings by His word. However, moving from the stage of thought to the stage of creation by the word is not a leap. Thought can be of various contents, but for that thought to be systematized and to aim for a single purpose and manifest in the form of the word, something new must be added; otherwise, it cannot develop further.

Not only is everything achieved by the word. There must be substantial content that can align with the word. In other words, some force must be applied to construct the substance based on the word. When viewed from the center of the word, this substance must be a more developed form of resurrection. Only in the presence of such a substance does joy arise. Furthermore, when joy arises, the work of harmony begins from there. Thus, when the manifested substance goes through a developmental process to a certain stage, love is finally applied there.

This is the form of the process by which God created the created beings. First, there was thought, then the word was added to form substance, and love is applied to that substance.

Through this creation process, all things were generated. When moving from the stage of thought to the stage of systematic word, that is, when one moves from a vague thought of how to create to attaching concrete content and forming a theoretical system in the form of the word, indescribable joy arises.

It is similar to when an artist expresses what he has envisioned in his work; seeing the completed work brings joy. Furthermore, when that work is made into a movie or a play and he gets to see it, a greater joy arises.

When what was thought in the heart is systematized theoretically, and based on that systematized theory, substance is formed, and that substance can relate to the whole, becoming the content of joy desired by the whole, then that substance becomes the most precious existence.

Therefore, when we look at humans today, we can think that God has infinitely strived to create one person centered on the ideal of the creation of heaven and earth. He thought about what process and in what form to create. Humans were also created by the word. Thus, as it is said, God decided to create humans in this form, with eyes like this, a nose like this, hands like this, and feet like this. Before creating humans, He sought a system that could explain that the form of humans would be like this, and then, based on that, connected the substantial beings to create humans.

When a human created as a single substance stands as a central being before all things, wouldn’t God be able to rejoice even more? There, the value of what God can rejoice in is determined. Adam served in such a position, and based on that, he created the sun and the moon. It is here that love is born. We know well that love is established in a place where the relative value is determined through a horizontal foundation.

What is the fastest way to approach God? 
When we think about this, what would be the path to approach God in relation to all things? Whether in society or family, what would be the way to get closer to God? Rather than vaguely trying to get closer to God, the fastest way is to trace the path that God has walked until now. If there were no such being as a person on this earth, how could one prove the position from which God thought to create humans?

God systematized and theorized His thoughts and created humans in the form He envisioned, and He wanted to pour His love into that person. From this perspective, we must understand that fallen humans are in a position where they must restore themselves.

Therefore, the most pressing issue for us is to know what kind of being we are rather than what we practice. Until today, history has flowed without clarifying the question of what kind of being humans are. Where do humans come from, and where are they going? We must clarify the question of what kind of being we are. To clarify that, we must seek the word of God and recreate the original form of humanity. We are currently ascending to that stage.

Today, the most pressing issue is to clarify what kind of being humans are rather than achieving the ideal world or utopian ideal that humans pursue. For fallen beings like us, the greatest issue is to clarify what kind of being I am. The problem is how to express this clarification through the word. This clarification has been the ultimate goal pursued by philosophy and religion until now. The question is how to prepare the form of the word that can clarify human existence and reveal it to the world.

Due to the fall of the human ancestors, humans have lost the connection to the substantialized relationship that was formed from God's thoughts to the form of the word. Therefore, you must seek to enter the word again. How far must you seek to enter? You must seek to the foundation of God's thoughts. In other words, you must seek to the conceptual realm that God envisioned through the word. Thus, you must reach the level where you can say, "Ah, this is what God was thinking." That path is the fastest way.

You must enter into God's thought realm and write God's substance through God's word and then come out again. Otherwise, you cannot achieve the ideal world from the fallen substance.

Therefore, when God created all things, He created them by the word, so you must reproduce the content of that word within yourself and find the form and system of the word that can relate to all substantial worlds within yourself. Then, will it end with finding the system of the word? No. You must go one step further and seek the thought of God from which the word originated, that is, you must seek to the realm of God's ideas. This is the problem.

The practice of meditation in Buddhism is also done to find the root of the mind. Therefore, they deny their sense of existence and pursue a state of nothingness. When one enters a state of nothingness, that is, when one completely loses the sense of existence of being born as a human, in other words, when one transcends the boundary of consciousness, one begins to relate to God's thought realm. By reaching such a state, a new idea that is not me is born. This newly born idea of mine will likely be a standard that is better than the current thoughts. This is what they pursue through meditation.

Similarly, what do you need here? It should not end with knowing these contents, but you must touch the foundation of the heart, that is, the foundation of thought. To do this, you must transcend all realities. Therefore, we must seek the path of deeply pursuing inwardly by unifying our spirit rather than extending outwardly. Isn’t this what is called prayer life in Christianity today? Wouldn’t it be more precious to pray to experience what God wants to say by connecting with God's thoughts than to set a goal and pray to fulfill it? That is why we seek a quiet place to pray.

The fundamental issue for being reborn as a new self 
Now you must relate to God by transcending all previous consciousness. Then, how vast will the range of being able to relate to God be? If you reach the level where God was thinking before creating heaven and earth, that range will touch infinity. And it will become a foundation that can encompass the entire world. Based on this, raising a new awareness is the starting point of creation and the origin of resurrection.

Just as God set a decisive standard saying, "I will do this," and resurrected humans, we must also establish a self-awareness standard that says, "I am like this," in a position that pursues infinite realms and decide that I must do this through systematic words. From there, the new second self is born.

When you discover yourself based on this foundation and feel your sense of existence from this standard, that self will be different from the self you have known until now. In other words, from there, an idea will arise that can participate in the position God is thinking from.

When you go out to witness in the local area and preach the word, you may have experienced that words come out of you without you even knowing. The human body is like a television or radio; as long as it has the relative conditions to resonate, it will definitely receive waves and resonate. Therefore, to resonate, one must have the property to completely match the frequency of those waves. Only then can one resonate.

Thus, it is necessary for us to have the attitude of reaching a state that is pure, clean, and calm. When that happens, one can align with the ideas that God thought of before creation. The relationship established through the word continues for eternity, so when our hearts come to know that realm, we can naturally reach a state that aligns with God's ideas.
You will enter, and from there, the wave of God's concept will come to you, and you will resonate with it. In other words, if you connect with the essence that has resonant elements, resonant results will inevitably appear. Realizing this position and moving forward with the purpose of the universe's creation that God desires, this person cannot help but become a new figure in the history of the substantial world.

Therefore, what is most important for us is how we will pursue the realm of God's thought, which is the foundation behind the words. This is the most important issue for us today. If you have listened to the words until now, you must act according to them from the day you heard them. If it is the Unification Church, you must move along the path of restoration centered on the principles of the Unification Church. You must start from a position where God's thoughts behind the words can be felt, allowing the words to take center stage. However, if you go out to evangelize from a position that is one step removed from God, maintaining a distance from Him, that is, from a position where you cannot relate to God, when you return, you will feel a sense of loss rather than joy, and you will feel that your results are poor. Such a person cannot last long.

Looking at the law of God's creation, that is, the process of creation, when the connection that can create two from one is established, God feels greater joy when two are created than when one is created. Can you feel joy when you see the substantial results you convey through the words, just as God feels joy?

When you convey the words based on the foundation of your own abilities, you will gradually feel a sense of loss. It does not develop into a world of joy but rather leads you to confront the end. Eventually, you will reach a state where you cannot contain yourself. The reason you are heading toward such a state now is that you do not have the original posture, that is, the posture aligned with God's thoughts when He began to speak at that time. Therefore, you inevitably reach such a conclusion.

So what is the problem here? Before going out with the words, you must embrace the words and strive to enter the inner realm of the words to align with the foundation of God's heart. This is the biggest issue. After that, you must move into the field where you can practice based on that foundation. When this heat begins to move, it will not be consumed as heat but will connect to the work of creating substantial authority that can correspond to a hundred.

For example, when electricity is generated at a power plant and sent to homes through transmission lines, the wires must be connected to the light bulb for it to shine at any time. Similarly, you cannot exert power without being connected to the source. Therefore, our fundamental issue is how we connect to the source. In other words, the biggest issue for us is God's heart.

However, fallen humanity is not in a position that can align with God's heart but is in a position that departs from God, seeking points of alignment in opposition to God. So where will you align with God? It must not be in the words. In other words, it should not be merely aligning with the words but must be aligned from the heart that is the source of the words. This is the issue you must pursue from now on.

To reach the realm where you can feel God's heart, what must you do? Prayer is necessary. For you, a life of prayer is the most important in that sense. When you engage in a life of prayer, indescribable joy comes. That realm is the realm of God's thoughts before the creation. If you can stand in a position where you can explain what you feel in that realm, isn't that the position God was in when He created heaven and earth? Isn't it the position where God created beings with His words? You must proclaim the words from such a realm. Then people will surely try to connect with those words.

The essence of love is such that it must resonate with nature, so when the true heart is moved, the object will inevitably seek to unify with it. Only when the object desires to be recreated as a substantial entity before the subject does development occur. From there, development centered on God becomes possible; it cannot happen with the words alone.

However, until now, you have received the words and lived without finding the roots of those words, merely thinking they are good. Therefore, rather than developing as time goes on, you have rather regressed more and more. If you continue like this, you may eventually lose God, and you may not even know if those words truly came from God, nor will you know how you relate to those words. If that happens, you will perish.

So why does this happen? Because God is the source of infinite power, there must be a creative work occurring in what is connected to that source, but the reason it does not happen lies in our inability to align with the principled standard. Therefore, fallen humanity has sought God's words until now. The history of humanity until now has been a history of pursuing truth.

Here, we Unification Church members must approach the foundation of God's heart behind the truth. When you enter such a position, an infinitely mysterious realm will unfold before you. And there, although it cannot be described in words, you will feel a power that transcends all the abilities of the world. Therefore, God exists. He is not absent. The question is whether you can reach such a realm.

You cannot go to that position if you are divided. You must be one to go. Therefore, the mind must be unified. When God created heaven and earth, He unified His mind before the words and pursued the world of ideals with one purpose. Likewise, you can gain joy by engaging in a life that connects with God's heart through the relative position of God.

The experience of prayer and joy does not come strongly all at once. It is felt through a state of being unsure whether it exists or not, through sensation, that is, inspiration. For example, when asked where the boundary between winter and spring is, it is said to be the beginning of spring, but even on the day of the beginning of spring, it is not clear whether it has transitioned from the winter season to the spring season. You do not know it if you are indifferent. It is like not knowing the difference between yesterday and today. Yet, it is not the same either. There is clearly a difference.

In the same way, if you have a spiritual entity, you must develop the property to connect with that spiritual entity and its foundation. You must completely develop it to establish a relationship where you can exchange feelings with God's heart. Before that, you must first feel whether such a spiritual entity exists or not. Even if that sensation is extremely weak, we must move forward based on it. You must never forget that feeling.

If you felt something yesterday, today you should build on that feeling and add today's feelings to it. Just as the four seasons of spring, summer, autumn, and winter revolve around the year, the world of the heart also naturally goes through the process of God's creation. Therefore, if you felt something at first, do not forget that sensation. It is absolutely essential within your realm of life, so you must strive to develop based on that feeling. This is why time for prayer is necessary. When you pray in such a realm, your prayers will be effective.

You will know when you pray. There are times when prayers go well. The human heart has the eye of the heart, that is, the spiritual eye, and there are times when the eye of God's heart and your heart's eye align perfectly. At that time, grace comes to you without you even realizing it. The issue is how to add to that feeling based on the experience in that mysterious realm.

If you receive such feelings through prayer, you will want to pray for a day instead of just one hour, and you will want to pray for three hours instead of two. The deeper you go, the greater the joy you will feel.

This is why the times for prayer vary with the seasons and differ among people. Some people pray at one in the morning, while others pray during the day. It varies from person to person. Therefore, you must seek the realm where your heart can resonate with God's heart. In that place, you must regard the feelings that come to you as absolute and treasure them more than anything in the world, holding onto them to find new joy.

The principle is that a perfect subject creates a perfect object. Therefore, when I save lives from a pure public position rather than a private one, the objects will testify. Thus, the objects will long for the subject, no matter how difficult the challenges they face. The reason young Unification Church members today yearn for the teacher is for this reason; they are in the position of a public subject.

You must recognize the need for prayer. Do you understand? "Yes." When you pray, you must not center on your selfish desires. You must pray from a more public perspective, from God's standpoint, for God. Even if it is difficult for you, you must do so. Sometimes, when we pray, we may suddenly say things we do not even know; that is God teaching us through all things.

Become a person who can taste the joy of the history of re-creation. When you do God's work, the birds fly, the rabbits hop, and the wind blows—all become God's teachings. At that time, everything uniformly becomes God's teachings. How can we express such a heaven and earth? How can we describe the feeling of flying into an infinite world, transcending time and space, while looking at a picturesque distant mountain? When you look at the flowing water in that realm, you will know where that water has flowed from and when. You understand the principle that droplets gather to form a stream.

God's world is a realm that transcends time and space. In contrast, history appears within the realm of realistic sensation. Likewise, even the largest things in the created world exist within the realm of realistic sensation. However, the contents of all phenomena that we can see and feel are infinite. Therefore, to feel such emotions, prayer is necessary. You must understand this.

When Jesus prayed, he prayed above all about how to transition to God's side. If you want to do the same, you must seek the foundation of God's heart, which is grieving in the original world. From there, you must practice with concrete content, that is, with the words. But have you practiced centered on the words? When you are connected to God's heart and establish substance centered on the words, you become in the same position as God, and the work of re-creation occurs. Do you understand? When the work of re-creation occurs, love proliferates. This is why offerings are necessary.

For example, if a patient is on the verge of death within an hour, and the doctor gives an injection that brings the patient back to life, the doctor feels joy and excitement in that moment. The liberation of one patient from death brings great joy to the doctor. Similarly, although there may be differences in height and depth, a country can be revived by a single leader in that sense.

The problem is that you have known the words, but you have not felt the joy of God's heart, that is, the joy and delight of a child being born. In other words, you have felt joy regarding the words, but you have not felt joy in your heart. This is why you need a life of prayer. The words are prepared, so you must feel the joy of the heart that God felt when He created and experienced, and only then will the work of re-creation appear. The power of love that allows God to govern heaven and earth is precisely the essence of the joy manifested in the creation process. You must understand that without adhering to this principle, you cannot expect the time of resurrection in the future.

Only when you taste the joy that others experience through your own restoration will you truly become a restored person. Do you understand? "Yes."

<Words> Humanity is in a position to decide whether the place they are currently living in is on the side of good or evil, centered on good and evil. Furthermore, whether I go in a good direction or an evil direction should not be determined by the power of a third party, but must be decided by my own judgment. We know this well. Moreover, as descendants of fallen humans who have not been able to bear the burden of responsibility, we must realize that we are at a critical crossroads where we must make this decision.

Human beings must be reborn by discerning good and evil. Because Adam failed to bear the burden of responsibility, we today are in a position where we cannot fulfill our mission without receiving help from anyone. The final decision is made by ourselves. In other words, the decision of whether to become a good person or an evil person is not made by God but must be made by ourselves.

What is the goal of human life, the standard of living? It is good. The center of this good is God. In other words, it is the Father. Therefore, we must understand that the one who determines whether I become a good person or an evil person centered on the One who is the center of goodness is none other than myself.

Thus, today, we must be reborn centered on the Father, grow anew, and go through the journey of life. In other words, we must be born through the Father, live through the Father, and die through the Father. And we must live with the Father in the eternal world. This is the path we must take today and the path of destiny we must follow in the future. 

In light of this, we fallen beings are not in a position of goodness. We are in a position of evil, which is the opposite of good due to the fall. Therefore, until now, I have undoubtedly been an evil person. Consequently, I was born from the lineage of evil and have lived in the environment of evil until now. 

Thus, because our past and present are evil, we are destined to have a future that is also evil. To escape from this, we must start a new life centered on the essence of goodness. In other words, we must be reborn. Thus, my journey of life must be divided into good and evil, and I must become the self that moves toward the good goal. Therefore, if the left side is evil and the right side is good on the path I am currently walking, I must go to the right, centered on good.

Therefore, I must feel that the new self born centered on goodness is more valuable and precious than the self that was born and lived evilly in the past. When I have the day to live in goodness, I must realize that I still have the destiny to indemnify the sins of the past when I look at the path of life I must walk in the future.

The individual is not formed solely from the reality of this self. I was born receiving the bloodline of countless ancestors throughout history, so I am like a secondary artifact. To return to the position of goodness with the new connection of life, I must have the new resolution and determination to step over the bloodline of my ancestors.

So what kind of position is that? It is a position where the power to deny evil and affirm good is strong enough to deny the entire past that is the origin of that nation. Only in such a position can we find the new connection of life.
It is through such connections that we will live a life of relationships, and from there, goodness arises and the expectations of goodness expand. This is the life of us who understand the meaning of broadening the expectations of goodness, and it is the path we must take in the future. We must understand this.

We must become people who form good relationships.
You must understand that the conscious "I" of today is different from the past "I." The relationships that can be formed today, centered on the conscious "I," must be more valuable than the relationships we had with brothers, relatives, nations, or the world in the past. In other words, we must form relationships with good parents, good siblings, good tribes, good nations, good countries, and good worlds. We must be aware of this. Even if we are aware of it, living for ourselves does not lead to goodness. Although we have awareness, our lives cannot be for ourselves. Those who feel this must become people who live for the past, for the present, and for the future. They must not only care for their own families but also live for the countless historical families, and for the families that will inherit the future nation and the world. Such people are needed. Furthermore, while living on behalf of their nation and country, they must not live for their own nation and country, but for the nations and countries of the future.

However, this has not clearly manifested in reality. Since it starts from us, if we do not live a good life centered on the conscious "I," we cannot form connections with a good world.

Why is that? Because until now, we have been formed by evil connections and have been immersed in an evil life, we must leave behind this evil connection centered on ourselves and establish a connection of God's creation that can expand beyond that in order to restore and indemnify. Indemnification means that if we suffer a loss of ten, we must establish some condition to bring back more than ten in profit for it to be considered indemnification. The indemnification we have done so far has been conditional indemnification. 

The condition of indemnification cannot be anything but a grateful grace to us. Ninety-five percent is God's responsibility, and five percent is human responsibility. While we may think of this as a formula, it is a very sad fact that we are doing conditional indemnification. In order to raise that conditional indemnification to a standard that is not conditional, God's effort and labor must be involved behind it. This is because we were born as descendants of fallen ancestors. Therefore, you must become people who can feel that we are too insufficient to stand before God. Thus, if there is someone who strives to seek a path of indemnification that is more than one hundred percent, this person can live a life that leaves a responsible foundation before God without fearing the conditions of indemnification.

Such a person can always dedicate and sacrifice themselves for the nation and the world. In other words, they are people who live with a heart of filial piety towards their families, a heart of loyalty towards their country, and a heart of sanctity towards the entire world. What kind of goal do such people live for? They do not live centered on the present self, looking forward to a day of victory, but live seeking the victory of the nation and the world. Therefore, they do not live for the satisfaction of the present but for the satisfaction of the future. Living for the future is a life that is in conflict with living for the present, so such people are rejected in reality, are lonely, and suffer losses. However, those who understand that this is something they must endure can overcome even the most difficult conditions of indemnification. We must understand this fact.

Looking at the life of Jesus, although it was a short life of about thirty years, he worked and lived for history and for the world. He lived in hope for the day when the banner of victory would be raised high, and because he lived with history and the world, all people cannot help but admire him. Jesus understood this, which is why he did not despair even when difficult circumstances blocked his path.

Good can eternally govern evil, but evil cannot eternally govern good. Evil may deceive or coercively govern good, but that is temporary. Good can never be eternally dominated by evil. If good were to be eternally dominated by evil, God's providence of restoration would be impossible.

We must be aware of ourselves before the Father.
When we look at God's providence of restoration, even if evil that opposed God was dominant for a time, that evil must inevitably become weak and ultimately hand over the foundation that was dominant over good. We can understand this through the historical process up to now. Likewise, even if good is currently dominated by evil, it will not be dominated forever. Ultimately, good will eternally govern evil.

Then, who becomes the absolute foundation that governs evil? It is neither God nor Satan. It is us humans. It is I. You must understand that God has been seeking this "I" until now. However, the "I" that God seeks must be a public "I," a person belonging to heaven. Only then can the relationship between the Father and the son be established. In other words, what God thinks is what I think, and what God does is what I must do. Therefore, thinking for God ultimately becomes thinking for myself, and the work for that becomes work for myself, and when we stand in a position where we realize this, we become people who have connections that God can be pleased with.

A minister who worries about what the king worries about and has the heart to solve that matter, claiming that it is their own work, can become a loyal subject. Likewise, when we look at it centered on the Father and me, the fact that the Father is worrying for me, that is, the Father is doing my work, is the issue of how I realize this. When I become aware of this, the Father and I can stand in one place. When that happens, the Father and I have one purpose, one life, and can fight against the enemy from one place. Without standing in such a position, we cannot live with the good God. Therefore, from now on, we must realize that we are newly born as people standing before the Father and that we must lead a new life from now on.

A life of faith that is grateful.
Until now, what God has worked hard for has ultimately been for me, and thinking that the 95 percent of the mission of the global pioneering path we must take from now on is also for me, we cannot help but be grateful to God.

Therefore, what is the essence of a life of faith? It is a heart of gratitude towards God. When such a heart exists, it becomes the foundation for overcoming the fallen relationship between God and me and forming one relationship.

Do I have to be in a good position in this world to be grateful? No. God has not only worked for us during good times until now. He has pledged to work even harder during difficult times. Therefore, in order for us to regard God as our Father today, we must be more grateful in difficult situations than in good situations, rather than simply thanking God from a good position. Thus, even on the heavy crossroad, it is possible to thank God when we understand this principle.

Among the countless people living on this earth, who is truly close to God in a meaningful way? It is those who, while living in the miserable conditions of underdeveloped countries, live with God, rather than those who walk the path of suffering in civilized nations or societies with cultural lives. If there are people who live with God even in such circumstances, they are not unhappy. There, the emotional connection with God is finally established.

The place where tears of joy and sorrow can coexist is not created in a place of play and leisure. It is created in a place of misery, bloodshed, and death. When we can meet in a place of indescribable misery, where tears intersect, and still give thanks, that is when we establish a connection with God. The new revolutionary flame and the new innovation movement have emerged from such places, centered on history. Therefore, when we seek to find a place where we can thank God, we must have the courage to be grateful not only in positions above our current lives but also in positions below them.

God has been in a position to save me until now, so He is more pitiful than I am. God is in a more pitiful position than I am. If a child is dying before their parents, of course, the child is pitiful, but the parents watching that child are even more pitiful. If the child, even in the place of dying, comforts the parents and expresses infinite gratitude, fulfilling their filial duty, they can fill the sorrow, pain, and misery of the parents.

In the same way, when we look at God and me, is it not God who is more pitiful than I am? When will there be a day when God can thank me? If God does not have a day to thank me, then no matter how much we thank God, that gratitude will only end with me and cannot bear fruit as gratitude centered on one purpose with God.

Then, what kind of position can God thank me more than I can? It is only the position of filial piety. So what is filial piety? It is when the child first feels sorrow for the parent's sorrow. At that time, the parent wants to regard that child as the embodiment of infinite hope, a being of value that replaces their entire life. In doing so, the parent thanks the child. The more difficult the circumstances, the more gratitude the parent will feel beyond necessity.

In light of this issue, we must think about how we can make the Father thank us in His presence. It is important to become such a person.

If we consider the morning, noon, evening, and night of a day as a microcosm of spring, summer, autumn, and winter, then morning corresponds to spring, noon to summer, evening to autumn, and night to winter. How can we live this day, which can replace the four seasons of the year, so that the Father can be grateful to us? This is the duty of filial piety and loyalty that we must fulfill before the Father.

From this perspective, when we wake up in the morning, we should pray that my daily life, as a representative of humanity, becomes the embodiment of gratitude before the Father, and that I will become the embodiment of hope that can be governed by the Father in a free garden like a spring garden in bloom. When it becomes noon and we go to work, we should aspire to become a being that can manifest value with God, like the growth of the embodiment of hope in the summer season. When evening comes, we should stand in a position to offer a single fruit to the Father, as it is a time like the autumn season when everything is gathered together. When it is night, corresponding to winter, we should become a being that can receive all energy by establishing an intrinsic relationship with God. If there is someone who can live a life of gratitude, making every day of the year a day of victory, they will feel that their life is meaningful in relation to the Father. Such a person will undoubtedly have such experiences and can spend their entire life in a life of gratitude. Even if such a person faces death, the heart of gratitude before God will remain.

We must live each day like this, each year like this, and throughout our lives like this. Our lives also have stages: childhood, youth, adulthood, and old age. This is similar to the morning, noon, evening, and night of a day, and the four seasons of a year. Therefore, only those who live their entire lives in this way can become victorious beings who fulfill the original purpose for which God created humanity.

Then, from where should we lay such a victorious foundation? When we look at a day, morning represents spring and infancy, noon represents summer and youth, evening represents autumn and adulthood, and night represents winter and old age. If there is someone who lives their life in gratitude in this manner, they are a person who cannot leave God. Such a person cannot escape from God's sight. We must think about the issue of whether such a person can escape from the environment that God protects.

The reason God leads us on the path of suffering.
Therefore, we must live a life of gratitude. I must critically examine my desires centered on the Father and consider whether those desires can bring joy to the Father. They must not conflict with the Father's position. To create a position that does not conflict with the Father's position, we must ascend through the history of restoration and indemnification, which requires walking the path of much suffering. Who should fill this path of suffering? We must not let God fill it; we must fill it ourselves. If my own strength is insufficient, I must mobilize my family, and if the strength of my family is insufficient, I must mobilize my tribe. I must become a person who strives to fulfill my responsibilities together with the strength of the mobilized family and tribe. Such a person, no matter how miserable their life may have been on this earth, will undoubtedly have lived centered on the Father, and thus can become a filial child and a loyal subject before the Father forever. You must understand this.

Therefore, we must become people who can live with a heart of gratitude that encompasses all sensations felt through the five senses and all intuitions felt through the heart. Since I was born from the Father, I must live with the Father and go before the Father. We must always realize that we are standing before the Father. It is difficult for anyone to be bound by anyone else while living. Even when faced with such difficult moments, we must never be bound by Satan but must be bound by God. And we must recognize the suffering given to us by God as a gift and joyfully accept it. We should not try to avoid suffering but confront it head-on. This path of suffering should be understood as a gift given by the Father, who loves me.

This becomes the motivation for me to become completely bound before God and to embark on a new world before any further difficulties arise in my life. Once I overcome this suffering, God will grant me a greater victorious foundation.
Yes. In order to make that victorious foundation relate to oneself, a condition of indemnity is necessary. Therefore, to relate to it, one must break through the sad and difficult environment that corresponds to it once again. This is God's operation to inherit a broader environment for me. Thus, we must live in a way that can embrace any suffering with joy. As such positions come closer to me, I must have the belief that these trials are coming so that the Father and I can become one, and I must become a person who can navigate through them. Such a person is a formidable individual. If there is a fearsome person in the world, there is no one more fearsome than this. There is no one who rebels against the satanic world on behalf of history more than this. From here, the satanic world will be subdued, and God's foundation will be expanded.

From this perspective, we must understand what kind of path of suffering the Unification Church must take in the future. The era of suffering centered on the family has passed. Today, we are in a position to establish a tribal environmental foundation among Unification Church members, so the path of suffering we must take has deviated from that. Now, before us, a greater force representing the evil powers will confront us. This is the existing nation and the existing world. This nation and world will confront us. We must not avoid the path of suffering that is coming but face it head-on, understanding it as the ultimate decisive condition for God to give us gifts, and we must become people who can accept this path of suffering with a heart of joy.

If there is someone who fights and wins from the standpoint of taking responsibility for this without entrusting it to anyone else, then on that foundation, no one else can stand but that person. However, if one reluctantly fights, wanting to escape, and finds themselves in a position of victory, God cannot give more blessings than that. Therefore, since I am already experiencing this, I must welcome it with joy, and even if there are more difficulties, I will go. I will fight. I will take responsibility. And with a heart of gratitude before God, I will say, "Tomorrow, please give me a thousandfold, ten thousandfold greater trials and entrust me with the path of your labor." When you entrust me with this work, is it not with a heart of apology? When this work is accomplished, it becomes a condition for the Father to be grateful. By doing this, a glorious position where the Father can be grateful will come to me. Knowing this fact, when I put forth my utmost effort to resolve that suffering, the conditions of filial piety and loyalty will be determined.

However, when one encounters such a position reluctantly, even if they create a position of victory in the environment, if a second or third condition of indemnity or path of suffering arises to inherit greater blessings, they will ultimately fail.

Be a person that God needs. We are already bodies that have prepared for death for the sake of the will. Then, in what position will we die? Dying for the sake of the individual is sorrowful. Dying for the sake of the family is also sorrowful. Dying for the sake of the tribe is sorrowful. Dying for the sake of the nation is also sorrowful. If we are to die for the sake of the will, is it not our desire to die for the sake of the world? If the distance to do so is far away, we must draw this world into our living stage to shorten that distance. There must be someone who dedicates all their intellect to fulfill that responsibility.

In the presence of the Father, God cannot help but rely on me if He cannot find the individual; He cannot help but rely on me if He cannot find the family; He cannot help but rely on me if He cannot find the tribe, nation, or state. When God can rely on me in this way, it means that my connection with God has been solidified.

The critical issue for you is how to have the self that can overcome the path of suffering with joy rather than sadness. Therefore, I must think about what I will do in the presence of the Father. Who am I looking at with my eyes now? Looking at my wife is to look at her in a free world; looking at my children is to look at them in the liberated kingdom; fighting and looking at the world today is to look at the world of tomorrow; and the efforts and sacrifices I make now are to transform into tomorrow's happiness and victory.

Everything I do, from sleeping to waking up, must be for the Father. All the important conditions of my life must be for the Father. I must live with gratitude before the Father... You must live from that standpoint. In such a position, I must not only be grateful myself, but I must also fulfill the conditions of indemnity. Shouldn't I bear a more weighted family condition of indemnity than a personal one? Only by fulfilling this will God be grateful. After fulfilling the family condition of indemnity, God will impose a national or tribal condition of indemnity upon me. If I can bear that, God will be grateful to me again. And He will impose a global condition of indemnity upon me. Why is that? Because it is humans who determine good and evil. God needs people, so He cannot help but entrust all global issues to me. God will elevate me. Therefore, we must not only long for that position but also look forward to the day when we fulfill our mission from that position.

The greater the position established for me, the greater the mission will be, and sorrow will come in proportion to that large scope, and likewise, the indemnity will come in proportion to that scope. Therefore, you must understand that unless you become a person who can joyfully welcome and be grateful for this content of indemnity, you cannot become a son who is praised before God.

The Unification Church must become a sacrificial offering. Today, we have become connected within the Unification Church. So, what is the Unification Church fighting for? It is not a church that fights for itself. You must understand that. The Unification Church is a church that fights for you, a church that fights for your family, a church that fights for your nation, and a church that fights for the world to come. In other words, it is like the offering placed on the altar. Who is this altar and offering for? It is for the world of hope to come. In other words, it is established to forgive those who have sinned. The Unification Church exists to forgive all wrongs of the world of death.

Then, it must bear more injustice than those who have sinned as a person without sin. This is the secret of indemnity. A pure person without sin must wear the mask of a sinner and sacrifice as if they were a sinner. 

If the sacrifice is for Satan, to whom will the result of the sacrifice be returned? It will not be returned to Satan but to oneself, as the sacrifice was made to fulfill God's purpose. At such times, one resurrects themselves. 

Jesus stood in such a position. Jesus stood as an offering and sacrificed for the nation and for sinners. And as a result of that sacrifice, God's will was fulfilled. The absolute standard by which Jesus' sacrifice could be fulfilled was that Jesus was resurrected as God's and was gathered with God through resurrection. Jesus did not only resurrect his own being. He had the content to gather the family, tribe, nation, and world, which is why new families, new tribes, new nations, and new worlds were born through Jesus, right?

So what does the Unification Church today aspire to be? It must become an offering from a denominational standpoint. When it becomes an offering, the issues change. Then, how do we reach that position? God must have conditions to boast about the Unification Church. To do that, we must not do it reluctantly but joyfully and gratefully do God's work. We must think that the trials coming before us are for the nation, the state, and the world. If I try to escape this path of suffering, I am not qualified to be a child of God.

Let us look forward to the 1970s with a heart of gratitude. Then, how do I discover the self that can be grateful? No matter what difficulties come to me from any village, I must regard them with gratitude and overcome the three-year crisis as I did the three-day journey. If you work hard for just three months from a position where you are not opposed in any village, that village will surely be grateful to you.

If I take on the path of suffering that the village must bear with a grateful heart and take responsibility, I will win, and those who are within that realm of victory will bow their heads to me. 

From this principle, we must recognize that as we look forward to the 1970s, the history of suffering is ending, and the era of the Unification Church's fortune is dawning, so we must know how to be grateful. Also, those who have never been grateful in the past must now strive to become a proud figure that God can establish by sacrificing everything, day or night, as we welcome this new era of fortune.

I do not need glory. Since God has paved the way of suffering until now, if there is someone who will now dedicate their life to the path of suffering with gratitude, that person will not perish. That person will surely be someone God will elevate and boast about.

If he moved for the nation, on the day that nation is found, he will become a child who can boast before that nation, and if he moved for the world, on the day the world is found, he will become a child who can boast before the world. God will elevate him and boast about him.

To do this, the Father must be able to express gratitude to you. Before you express gratitude, God must first be able to say thank you to you. When God stands in a position where He can say thank you, He will mobilize spiritual people or good ancestors to support that person and make them grateful and bow their heads. You must understand that this is the content of restoration.

From this perspective, a group of gratitude centered around Kim Sung-do, the mother of Jeong Seok-on, has emerged among the new sects of Korean Christianity today. This fact raises our awareness of our faith life. We must recognize that they have come out to represent an absolute group that must complete a life of gratitude. Therefore, we must be grateful in every circumstance.

When you become such individuals and pledge to dedicate your lives before the Father, even if you are in death, God will resurrect you and boast about you in the heavenly world. 

Do not lament that you are not recognized in the world and that you cannot accomplish worldly matters. We are centered on eternal will, so we must establish conditions of indemnity that God requires in relation to that eternal will, and we must fulfill the work that God desires with gratitude. Therefore, if we can leave a connection that allows the Father to be grateful, we will never perish. Thus, you must know that if you do not return to your local area and live this way, you cannot fulfill your mission.

When you step onto the altar, you must do so with a heart of gratitude. Even if you are selling something, you must approach the sale with a heart of gratitude. The condition of thinking, "I am in difficulty now, so I can do this and that," will not work. You must understand that you have a destiny that cannot be comfortable until God is comfortable. And because you are in a position to serve the Father, it is principled that you must suffer more than the Father. From this perspective, there are many things that the district leaders and regional leaders today have not been able to take responsibility for.

We must always be aware that we are in the presence of the Father. Because I am in the presence of the Father, He knows what I am thinking right now, what I am trying to do, and He observes all my feelings and senses. If I leave only the standard of gratitude here, your path will progress rapidly.

From this perspective, I hope to leave a good motive for re-launching towards the 1970s by reflecting on the past.

<Prayer> Father! If we are sons who know your sincerity, we cannot help but bow down with a heart that cannot hide the shameful appearance of a sinner, even if we wake up from sleep. 

At the breakfast table, may I become a self that asks myself what I will do after eating this meal, and when I face the lunch table, may I become a self that reflects on what I have left until now with a shameful appearance. And when I face the dinner table, may I become a self that can ask whether I have spent a day that is sufficient to settle the day.

Have I started the day with what belongs to the Father and come this far with what belongs to the Father? And when I think about how much interest the Father has in me, I must reflect on whether I have spent a day that is valuable but left nothing behind, and as I lie down in bed, I must feel regret and be a child who can repent before the Father with tears.

We must live a life of gratitude. Even in the place of being beaten, even in the place of bleeding, we must live a life of gratitude. Because many ancestors betrayed the Father in such places, we are those who must fulfill the duty of filial piety among filial piety and the duty of loyalty among loyalty. Here, let us understand that we cannot stand in that position with resentment and complaints, and let us become those who are afraid of discovering such selves. Though we may be pitiful and weak in the world, let us understand that there is no one more fearsome than such a person. 

Let us become sons who can live there with the compassion of the Father and who cannot stand before the Father without receiving the compassion to the extent that the Father can recommend that someone love me through many ancestors in the spirit world. 

Therefore, let us be able to accept everything with a heart of gratitude, and even if my body is in a position where it cannot sustain itself, let us think that the Father overcame a path of suffering even more severe than this while longing for me. I must discover the fact that only by overcoming this suffering can I become a son who can comfort the Father's sorrowful past, and I must separate myself to become a son who is completely offered as a sacrifice before the Father.

We have nothing but to live a life of gratitude. Even if the wife bound to one man is lacking, I must be grateful for the fact that there is something through which I can serve her throughout my life. Even if a child gives me a life of the cross, I must be grateful for the fact that I have been given the opportunity to prepare for that. Even if the environment drives me into a pit of despair where I cannot sustain my life, I must become a son who can leave that as a condition of gratitude and say that I will fall, and I earnestly hope to be a person of the Father.
I wish to ask.
We have a responsibility to place our nation before us. Furthermore, I know that there are paths beyond the suffering that families endure. I believe that the difficulties in my life are only temporary. When I think about the national suffering that still lies ahead, I realize that we must adopt a brave attitude to overcome it.

Once we surpass the national suffering we must bear, there awaits a path of global suffering that is thousands of times greater, but it is our destiny to walk this path, and we must understand that if we cannot walk it while alive, we must do so even in death. Therefore, may we always be able to face any suffering with gratitude, and may we be granted the attitude of sons before the Father. Otherwise, I know that the Father will have no choice but to shed tears of lamentation for me. Even if I must tread the path of disgrace and death, I earnestly ask and wish to be a son who offers himself for the Father and becomes a loyal subject.

Father, please bless the year 1970. From now on, may the children of unification be granted the ability to be grateful in their hearts, and regardless of any commands from above, may they run according to those commands and maintain a grateful heart even when they fall in their efforts. May we be children who can boast that the place where we hold onto the Father and pray is a point of honor that cannot be traded for anything in life.

In the 1970s, may I become a son who is worthy of entrusting the fortunes of heaven, and may a daughter be raised above that son so that the family receives the blessings of the Father. I earnestly ask and wish for this.

May this period become a special time for us, preparing a new promise for tomorrow, and for the glory of the Father, may we be heavenly soldiers who hold the shield of victory and run bravely as heavenly warriors. I ask for this while offering all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
